# <a name="quality-of-experience-review-guide"></a><span data-ttu-id="73324-103">體驗品質的審查指南</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-103">Quality of Experience Review Guide</span></span>

<!-- Note that this link to the Word doc is intentionally NOT the aka.ms/qerquide link -->
<span data-ttu-id="73324-104">本指南針對 Microsoft 團隊和商務用 Skype Online 的 [磁片磁碟機值] 階段。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-104">This guide is about the Drive Value phase for Microsoft Teams and Skype for Business Online.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-105">您可以下載本指南的[Word 版本](https://github.com/MicrosoftDocs/OfficeDocs-SkypeForBusiness/blob/live/Teams/downloads/quality-of-experience-review-guide.docx?raw=true)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-105">You can [download a Word version](https://github.com/MicrosoftDocs/OfficeDocs-SkypeForBusiness/blob/live/Teams/downloads/quality-of-experience-review-guide.docx?raw=true) of this guide.</span></span>

## <a name="introduction"></a><span data-ttu-id="73324-106">簡介</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-106">Introduction</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-107">若要對改善使用者體驗帶來最大的影響，組織必須 operationalize 下圖所示的主要區域。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-107">To have the greatest impact on improving the user experience, organizations need to operationalize the key areas that are shown in the following figure.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-108">其他區域包括識別操作工作、針對品質指標建立目標、ascertaining 度量組織成功的標準，以及視需要將調查區域縮小。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-108">Additional areas include identifying operational tasks, establishing targets for quality metrics, ascertaining the metrics to use to gauge organizational success, and narrowing areas of investigation as needed.</span></span>


<span data-ttu-id="73324-109">![使用者體驗品質的主要區域](media/qerguide-image-keyareas.png "使用者經驗品質的主要區域包括音訊、可靠性、使用者問卷、裝置和用戶端。")</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-109">![Key areas for the quality of user experience](media/qerguide-image-keyareas.png "Key areas for the quality of user experience include audio, reliability, user surveys, devices, and clients.")</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-110">_圖 1-本指南涵蓋的主要操作區域_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-110">_Figure 1 - Key operational areas covered throughout this guide_</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-111">透過連續評估與修正本指南中所述的區域，您可以減少對使用者體驗品質產生負面影響的可能性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-111">By continually assessing and remediating the areas described in this guide, you can reduce their potential to negatively affect the quality of your users’ experience.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-112">在部署中遇到的大多數使用者體驗問題，都可以分為下列類別：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-112">Most user-experience problems encountered in a deployment can be grouped into the following categories:</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="73324-113">防火牆或 proxy 配置不完整</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-113">Incomplete firewall or proxy configuration</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="73324-114">低 wi-fi 覆蓋範圍</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-114">Poor Wi-Fi coverage</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="73324-115">頻寬不足</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-115">Insufficient bandwidth</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="73324-116">點對點</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-116">VPN</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="73324-117">用戶端版本與驅動程式不一致或過時</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-117">Inconsistent or outdated client versions and drivers</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="73324-118">未優化或內建音訊裝置</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-118">Unoptimized or built-in audio devices</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="73324-119">有問題的子網或網路裝置</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-119">Problematic subnets or network devices</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-120">在部署團隊或商務用 Skype Online 前，請先進行適當的規劃與設計，您就可以減少維持高品質體驗所需的工作量。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-120">Through proper planning and design before deploying Teams or Skype for Business Online, you can reduce the amount of effort that will be required to maintain high-quality experiences.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-121">本指南的重點是使用 [通話品質儀表板] （CQD）線上作為主要工具來報告及調查每一個區域，並在音訊上特別強調最大化採納與影響。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-121">This guide focuses on using the Call Quality Dashboard (CQD) Online as the primary tool to report and investigate each area, with a special emphasis on audio to maximize adoption and impact.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-122">針對改善音訊體驗的網路所做的任何改善，也會直接翻譯成影片與桌面共用的改良功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-122">Any improvements made to the network to improve the audio experience will also directly translate to improvements in video and desktop sharing.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-123">為加速您的評估，提供[兩個策劃 CQD 範本](https://aka.ms/qertemplates)：一個用於管理所有網路，而另一個則只針對受管理（內部）網路篩選。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-123">To accelerate your assessment, [two curated CQD templates](https://aka.ms/qertemplates) are provided: one is for managing all networks and the other is filtered for managed (internal) networks only.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-124">雖然所有網路範本報告都設定為顯示建立和網路資訊，但是當您在收集與上傳資訊時，仍然可以使用它們。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-124">Although the All Networks template reports are configured to display building and network information, they can still be used while you work toward collecting and uploading building information.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-125">將組建資訊上傳到 CQD，可讓服務在與外部子網區分內部的同時，透過新增自訂的建築物、網路和位置資訊來加強報告。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-125">Uploading building information into CQD enables the service to enhance reporting by adding custom building, network, and location information while differentiating internal from external subnets.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-126">如需詳細資訊，請參閱本指南稍後的[建立對應](#building-mapping)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-126">For more information, see [Building mapping](#building-mapping) later in this guide.</span></span>

### <a name="intended-audience"></a><span data-ttu-id="73324-127">目標物件</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-127">Intended audience</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-128">本指南專供合作夥伴與客戶干係人使用，其中包含共同作業主管/架構師、顧問、變更管理/採納專家、支援/技術支援人員、網路組長、桌面組長及 IT 系統管理員等角色。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-128">This guide is intended to be used by partner and customer stakeholders with roles such as Collaboration Lead/Architect, Consultant, Change Management/Adoption Specialist, Support/Help Desk Lead, Network Lead, Desktop Lead, and IT Admin.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-129">本指南也專供指定的品質擁護者使用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-129">This guide is also intended to be used by the designated quality champion(s).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-130">如需詳細資訊，請參閱[品質擁護者角色](4-envision-plan-my-service-management.md#the-quality-champion-role)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-130">For more information, see [the Quality Champion role](4-envision-plan-my-service-management.md#the-quality-champion-role).</span></span>

## <a name="prerequisites"></a><span data-ttu-id="73324-131">先決條件</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-131">Prerequisites</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-132">使用本指南前，請確定您已指派適當的租使用者[角色](https://docs.microsoft.com/office365/admin/add-users/about-admin-roles)，以便存取 CQD。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-132">Before using this guide, make sure you have the proper tenant [roles](https://docs.microsoft.com/office365/admin/add-users/about-admin-roles) assigned so that you can access CQD.</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="73324-133">**Office 365 全域系統管理員**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-133">**Office 365 Global Administrator**</span></span> 

-   <span data-ttu-id="73324-134">**商務用 Skype 系統管理員**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-134">**Skype for Business Administrator**</span></span> 

-   <span data-ttu-id="73324-135">**Teams 服務管理員**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-135">**Teams Service Administrator**</span></span> 

-   <span data-ttu-id="73324-136">**Teams 通訊系統管理員**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-136">**Teams Communications Administrator**</span></span> 

-   <span data-ttu-id="73324-137">**Teams 通訊支援工程師**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-137">**Teams Communications Support Engineer**</span></span> 

-   <span data-ttu-id="73324-138">**團隊溝通支援專家**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-138">**Teams Communications Support Specialist**</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="73324-139">或者，您可以將下列角色指派給 Office 365 使用者帳戶，只允許存取報告功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-139">Alternatively, you can assign the following role to an Office 365 user account to allow access to reporting features only.</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="73324-140">**報告閱讀程式：** 可以在系統管理中心中查看所有[活動報告](https://support.office.com/article/activity-reports-0d6dfb17-8582-4172-a9a9-aed798150263)、 [Microsoft 365 採用內容套件](https://support.office.com/article/Office-365-Adoption-content-pack-77ff780d-ab19-4553-adea-09cb65ad0f1f)中的任何報告，以及 CQD 報告。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-140">**Reports Reader:** Can view all the [activity reports](https://support.office.com/article/activity-reports-0d6dfb17-8582-4172-a9a9-aed798150263) In the admin center, any reports from the [Microsoft 365 Adoption content pack](https://support.office.com/article/Office-365-Adoption-content-pack-77ff780d-ab19-4553-adea-09cb65ad0f1f), and CQD reports.</span></span>

## <a name="what-is-quality"></a><span data-ttu-id="73324-141">什麼是品質？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-141">What is quality?</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-142">當您在小組和商務用 Skype 中討論品質時，請務必定義一個術語來達成共同的認識。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-142">When discussing quality in Teams and Skype for Business, it’s important to define the term to achieve a common understanding.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-143">如這裡所定義的品質，是服務規格與使用者經驗的結合。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-143">Quality, as defined here, is a combination of service metrics and user experience.</span></span>

<!-- Note: need to update graphic-->
<span data-ttu-id="73324-144">![服務度量和使用者體驗的圖例](media/qerguide-image-whatisquality.png "Service 量度是由資料流程比例差、可靠性、端點/裝置和用戶端版本所組成。使用者體驗是由使用者對服務品質的感覺所組成。」)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-144">![Illustration of service metrics and the user experience](media/qerguide-image-whatisquality.png "Service metrics are made up of poor stream ratio, reliability, endpoints/devices, and client versions. The user experience is made up of the user's perception of the quality of the service.")</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-145">_圖 2-什麼是品質？_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-145">_Figure 2 - What is quality?_</span></span>

### <a name="service-metrics"></a><span data-ttu-id="73324-146">服務度量單位</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-146">Service metrics</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-147">服務度量單位是由特定的用戶端測量標準所組成。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-147">Service metrics consist of specific client-based metrics.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-148">在每次通話期間，用戶端會收集通話的遙測資訊，並在每次通話結束後提交報告，以便日後可透過 CQD 或[呼叫分析](https://techcommunity.microsoft.com/t5/Skype-for-Business-Blog/Introducing-Call-Analytics/ba-p/57309)進行存取。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-148">During each call, the client collects telemetry information about the call and submits a report at the end of each call that can be later accessed through CQD or [Call Analytics](https://techcommunity.microsoft.com/t5/Skype-for-Business-Blog/Introducing-Call-Analytics/ba-p/57309).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-149">這些指標包括：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-149">These metrics include:</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="73324-150">較差的串流速率</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-150">Poor Stream Rate</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="73324-151">設定失敗率</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-151">Setup Failure Rate</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="73324-152">丟單失敗率</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-152">Drop Failure Rate</span></span>


#### <a name="poor-stream-rate"></a><span data-ttu-id="73324-153">較差的串流速率</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-153">Poor Stream Rate</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-154">較差的串流速率（PSR.EXE）代表組織中品質較差的資料流程總百分比。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-154">The poor stream rate (PSR) represents the organization’s overall percentage of streams that have poor quality.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-155">這個指標是要醒目提示貴組織在哪些區域中，您的組織能專注于減少此值並改善使用者體驗等最大的影響，這就是為什麼在查看 PSR.EXE 時， [managed 網路](#managed-vs-unmanaged-networks)是主要的焦點。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-155">This metric is meant to highlight areas where your organization can concentrate effort to have the strongest impact toward reducing this value and improving the user experience, which is why [managed networks](#managed-vs-unmanaged-networks) are the primary focus when looking at PSR.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-156">外部使用者也很重要，但調查會因組織而異。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-156">External users are important too, but investigation differs on an organizational basis.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-157">考慮為外部使用者提供最佳做法，並獨立于整體組織調查外部通話。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-157">Consider providing best practices for external users, and investigate external calls independently from the overall organization.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-158">CQD 中的實際度量單位依工作負載而有所不同，但為了讓品質體驗進行評審，我們主要將重點放在_音訊不佳的百分比_測量中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-158">The actual measurement in CQD varies by workload, but for the purposes of the Quality Experience Review we focus primarily on the _Audio Poor Percentage_ measurement.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-159">PSR.EXE 是由下表所述的五個網路度量值所組成。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-159">PSR is made up of the five network metric averages described in the following table.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-160">針對要分類為較差的資料流程，只有一個公制需要超過定義的閾值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-160">For a stream to be classified as poor, only one metric needs to exceed the defined threshold.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-161">如需有關資料流程分類程式的詳細資訊，請參閱[這篇文章](stream-classification-in-call-quality-dashboard.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-161">For more information about the stream classification process, see [this article](stream-classification-in-call-quality-dashboard.md).</span></span>

> [!Note]
> <span data-ttu-id="73324-162">CQD 提供「不佳的原因 ...」</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-162">CQD provides the “Poor Due To…”</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-163">測量，以更清楚地瞭解哪個條件導致資料流程分類為較差。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-163">measurements to better understand what condition caused the stream to be classified as poor.</span></span>


<span data-ttu-id="73324-164">_表格 1-音訊品質不佳的指標_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-164">_Table 1 - Audio poor quality metrics_</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="73324-165">公制平均值</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-165">Metric average</span></span>     | <span data-ttu-id="73324-166">描述</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-166">Description</span></span>     | <span data-ttu-id="73324-167">使用者體驗</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-167">User experience</span></span> |
|-------------|-----------------|-----------------|
| <span data-ttu-id="73324-168">抖動\>30 毫秒</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-168">Jitter \>30 ms</span></span>        | <span data-ttu-id="73324-169">這是連續資料包之間延遲的平均變更。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-169">This is the average change in delay between successive packets.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-170">團隊和商務用 Skype 可透過緩衝來適應某些層級的抖動。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-170">Teams and Skype for Business can adapt to some levels of jitter through buffering.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-171">只有抖動超過參與者通知抖動效果的緩衝時才是如此。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-171">It’s only when the jitter exceeds the buffering that a participant notices the effects of jitter.</span></span>      | <span data-ttu-id="73324-172">以不同速度傳入的資料包會導致演講者的語音音效機器人。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-172">The packets arriving at different speeds cause a speaker’s voice to sound robotic.</span></span>   |
| <span data-ttu-id="73324-173">資料包遺失率\>10% 或0。1</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-173">Packet loss rate \>10% or 0.1</span></span>        | <span data-ttu-id="73324-174">這通常會定義為遺失的資料包百分比。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-174">This is often defined as a percentage of packets that are lost.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-175">資料包遺失會直接影響音訊品質-從較小、個別的遺失包，這些資料包幾乎不會影響到導致音訊完全剪下的後置脈衝損失。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-175">Packet loss directly affects audio quality—from small, individual lost packets that have almost no impact to back-to-back burst losses that cause audio to cut out completely.</span></span>     | <span data-ttu-id="73324-176">丟棄且未送達預期目的地的資料包會引起媒體中的差距，導致不想要的音節與單字，以及不連貫的影片和共用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-176">The packets being dropped and not arriving at their intended destination cause gaps in the media, resulting in missed syllables and words, and choppy video and sharing.</span></span> |
| <span data-ttu-id="73324-177">雙程時間\>500 ms</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-177">Round-trip time \>500 ms</span></span>        | <span data-ttu-id="73324-178">這是取得從 A 指向點 B 並回到點 A 的 IP 資料包所需的時間。此網路傳播延遲會與兩個點之間的物理距離和光線速度之間的距離相關，並包括網路路徑中各種裝置所佔用的額外額外負荷。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-178">This is the time it takes to get an IP packet from point A to point B and back to point A. This network propagation delay is tied to the physical distance between the two points and the speed of light, and includes additional overhead taken by the various devices in the network path.</span></span>      | <span data-ttu-id="73324-179">資料包太長而無法送達目的地會導致 walkie talkie 的效果。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-179">The packets taking too long to arrive at their destination cause a walkie-talkie effect.</span></span>   |
| <span data-ttu-id="73324-180">NMOS 下降平均值\>1。0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-180">NMOS degradation average \>1.0</span></span>         | <span data-ttu-id="73324-181">資料流程的平均[網路平均觀念成績（NMOS）](https://docs.microsoft.com/previous-versions/office/communications-server/bb894481(v=office.12)#network-mos)下降。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-181">Average [Network Mean Opinion Score (NMOS)](https://docs.microsoft.com/previous-versions/office/communications-server/bb894481(v=office.12)#network-mos) degradation for the stream.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-182">代表網路遺失和抖動對導致 NMOS 下降的音訊品質有多大的影響。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-182">Represents how much the network loss and jitter has affected the quality of received audio that caused the NMOS to drop by more than one point.</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="73324-183">這會結合抖動、資料包遺失，以及較低的程度，增加往返時間。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-183">This is a combination of jitter, packet loss, and—to a lesser degree—increased round-trip time.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-184">使用者可能會遇到這些問題的組合。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-184">The user might be experiencing a combination of these symptoms.</span></span>   |
| <span data-ttu-id="73324-185">隱藏樣本\>7% 或0.07 的平均比率</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-185">Average ratio of concealed samples \>7% or 0.07</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="73324-186">音訊幀數的平均比率，由資料包遺失修複產生的隱藏範例，到音訊畫面總數目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-186">Average ratio of the number of audio frames with concealed samples generated by packet loss healing to the total number of audio frames.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-187">隱藏的音訊範例是一種技術，用來平滑通常是由網路資料包所造成的突然轉場。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-187">A concealed audio sample is a technique used to smooth out the abrupt transition that would usually be caused by dropped network packets.</span></span>      | <span data-ttu-id="73324-188">[高值] 表示已套用大量的 [損失 concealment]，並產生扭曲或遺失的音訊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-188">High values indicate that significant levels of loss concealment were applied and resulted in distorted or lost audio.</span></span>     |

#### <a name="setup-failure-rate"></a><span data-ttu-id="73324-189">設定失敗率</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-189">Setup Failure Rate</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-190">設定失敗率（亦即在 CQD 中的_呼叫設定失敗百分比_測量）是在通話開始時端點之間無法建立媒體路徑的串流數。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-190">The setup failure rate, otherwise known as the _Total Call Setup Failure Percentage_ measurement in CQD, is the number of streams where the media path couldn’t be established between the endpoints at the start of the call.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-191">這代表無法建立的任何媒體資料流程。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-191">This represents any media stream that couldn’t be established.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-192">根據此處測量的使用者經驗影響的嚴重性，目標是將此值縮小至盡可能接近零。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-192">Given the severity of the impact on the user experience measured here, the goal is to reduce this value to as close to zero as possible.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-193">這個指標的高值在新部署中的防火牆規則不完整的情況下比較常見，但請務必定期觀看。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-193">A high value for this metric is more common in new deployments with incomplete firewall rules than a mature deployment, but it’s still important to watch on a regular basis.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-194">這個指標是透過取得失敗的資料流程總數除以提交成功呼叫詳細資料記錄（CDR）的總串流數來計算：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-194">This metric is calculated by taking the total number of streams that failed to set up divided by the total number of streams that submitted a successful call detail record (CDR):</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="73324-195">**設定失敗率**= 總的通話設定失敗資料流程計數/總 CDR 可用資料流程計數</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-195">**Setup Failure Rate** = Total Call Setup Failed Stream Count / Total CDR Available Stream Count</span></span>

#### <a name="drop-failure-rate"></a><span data-ttu-id="73324-196">丟單失敗率</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-196">Drop Failure Rate</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-197">在 CQD 中，擊落失敗率（亦稱為 [_總呼叫中斷失敗百分比_]）是已成功建立的資料流程在媒體路徑無法正常終止的百分比。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-197">The drop failure rate, otherwise known as the _Total Call Dropped Failure Percentage_ measurement in CQD, is the percentage of successfully established streams where the media path didn’t terminate normally.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-198">這代表任何意外終止的媒體資料流程。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-198">This represents any media stream that terminated unexpectedly.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-199">雖然這種影響並不像是無法設定的資料流程那樣嚴重，但會對使用者體驗造成負面影響。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-199">Although the impact of this isn’t as severe as a stream that failed to set up, it will negatively affect the user experience.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-200">突然且頻繁的媒體跌落不只會對使用者體驗產生嚴重影響，因此它們會導致使用者需要重新連線，進而導致生產率損失。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-200">Sudden and frequent media drops not only can have a severe impact on the user experience, they result in the need for users to reconnect, resulting in a loss in productivity.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-201">指標的計算方式為：將丟棄的資料流程總數除以已成功設定的資料流程總計數：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-201">The metric is calculated by taking the total number of dropped streams divided by the total count of streams that set up successfully:</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="73324-202">**丟單失敗率**= 總的呼叫中斷串流總數/總呼叫設定成功的資料流程計數</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-202">**Drop Failure Rate** = Total Call Dropped Stream Count / Total Call Setup Succeeded Stream Count</span></span>

### <a name="define-your-target-metrics"></a><span data-ttu-id="73324-203">定義您的目標度量</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-203">Define your target metrics</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-204">本節討論我們用來評估服務體驗狀況的一些核心服務度量單位。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-204">This section discusses some of the core service metrics that we use to assess how services experience health.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-205">若要不斷地評估並推動努力，將這些測量標準放在其定義的目標之下，您將有助於確保您的使用者體驗一致且可靠的通話品質。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-205">By continually assessing and driving efforts to keep these metrics below their defined targets, you’ll help ensure that your users experience consistent, reliable call quality.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-206">若要開始使用，我們提供下列目標。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-206">To get you started, the following targets are provided.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-207">_資料表 2-核心目標狀況評估指標_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-207">_Table 2 - Core target health assessment metrics_</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-261">討論與定義貴組織的目標以符合您的業務目標，這一點非常重要。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-261">It's important to discuss and define your organization’s targets to meet your business objectives.</span></span>

### <a name="user-experience"></a><span data-ttu-id="73324-262">使用者體驗</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-262">User experience</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-263">分析使用者體驗的美工圖案比科學更多，因為這裡收集的度量單位並不一定代表網路或服務發生問題，而是只指示使用者感覺問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-263">Analyzing the user experience is more art than science, because the metrics gathered here don’t always mean that there’s a problem with the network or service but rather, they simply indicate that the user perceives a problem.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-264">Microsoft 提供內建的調查機制（稱為「評定我的通話比率（RMC）」），協助估量總體使用者體驗。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-264">Microsoft offers a built-in survey mechanism—known as Rate My Call (RMC)—to help gauge overall user experience.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-265">RMC 將會協助您從使用者的觀點回答下列問題：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-265">RMC will help you answer the following questions from your users’ perspective:</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="73324-266">我知道如何使用此方案嗎？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-266">Do I know how to use the solution?</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="73324-267">這個方案便於使用且直觀，而且它支援我的日常通訊需求？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-267">Is the solution easy to use and intuitive, and does it support my day-to-day communication needs?</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="73324-268">此方案可協助我完成工作嗎？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-268">Does the solution help me get my job done?</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="73324-269">這個方案的整體認識是什麼？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-269">What’s my overall perception of the solution?</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="73324-270">無論是在何處，都能在任何時間點使用解決方案？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-270">Can I use the solution at any point in time, regardless of where I am?</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="73324-271">我可以設定及維護通話嗎？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-271">Can I set up and maintain a call?</span></span>

#### <a name="rate-my-call"></a><span data-ttu-id="73324-272">評價我的通話</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-272">Rate My Call</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="73324-273">[評級我的通話] （RMC）會內置在團隊和商務用 Skype 中，而且會自動設定為在每10個通話中有一人或10% 時顯示給參與者。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-273">Rate My Call (RMC) is built into Teams and Skype for Business and is automatically configured to be displayed to the participant after one in every 10 calls, or 10 percent.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-274">此簡短問卷會要求使用者對通話進行評分，並提供一些內容，以瞭解為何通話品質可能較差。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-274">This brief survey asks the user to rate the call and provide a little context for why the call quality might have been poor.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-275">一或兩個評等不佳，3到4個是良好的，5是極好的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-275">A one or two rating is considered poor, three to four is good, and five is excellent.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-276">雖然這是延遲指標的一部分，但對於發現服務規格可能遺漏的問題而言，這是一個非常實用的規格。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-276">Although it’s somewhat of a lagging indicator, this is a useful metric for uncovering issues that service metrics can miss.</span></span>

> [!Note]
> <span data-ttu-id="73324-277">除非使用者透過提供良好的意見反應來回應 RMC 問卷，否則回應通常會傳回 overwhelmingly 否定。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-277">Until users are educated to respond to RMC surveys by giving good feedback in addition to bad, responses typically come back as overwhelmingly negative.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-278">大多數的使用者只會在通話品質較差時回應。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-278">Most users only respond when call quality is poor.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-279">因此，即使服務度量良好，您的 RMC 報告也可能會在差側扭曲。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-279">Because of this, your RMC reports might be skewed to the poor side even while service metrics are good.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-280">您可以使用 CQD 來報告 RMC 的使用者回應，並將範例報告包含在 CQD 範本中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-280">You can use CQD to report on RMC user responses, and sample reports are included in the CQD template.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-281">不過，本指南中不會詳細討論它們。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-281">However, they aren’t discussed in detail in this guide.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-282">如需在商務用 Skype Online 中 RMC 的詳細資訊，以及教育使用者提供實用 RMC 回應的指導方針，請參閱[這篇博客文章](https://blogs.technet.microsoft.com/jenstr/2015/05/05/rate-my-call-in-skype-for-business-2015/)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-282">For more information about RMC in Skype for Business Online and guidance for educating users to give useful RMC responses, see [this blog post](https://blogs.technet.microsoft.com/jenstr/2015/05/05/rate-my-call-in-skype-for-business-2015/).</span></span>

#### <a name="client-and-device-readiness"></a><span data-ttu-id="73324-283">用戶端和裝置準備就緒</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-283">Client and device readiness</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-284">您需要實體用戶端和裝置策略，以協助確保您的使用者擁有一致且積極的使用者體驗。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-284">You need a solid client and device strategy to help ensure that your users have a consistent and positive user experience.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-285">幾個主要原則會推動每個準備策略。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-285">A few key principles drive each readiness strategy.</span></span>

##### <a name="client-readiness"></a><span data-ttu-id="73324-286">用戶端就緒</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-286">Client readiness</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-287">強有力的用戶端準備策略可確保您的使用者能夠在享有最佳體驗的情況下執行最新版的用戶端。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-287">A strong client readiness strategy ensures that your users are running the most recent version of the client while enjoying the best experience possible.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-288">Microsoft 定期為商務用 Skype 用戶端修補程式;確保您的環境中的最新資料保持在最新狀態，對於您的整體成功至關重要。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-288">Microsoft routinely patches the Skype for Business client; ensuring that you keep it up to date in your environment is vital to your overall success.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-289">請務必記住修補網路、影片、USB 和音訊驅動程式，因為它們經常被忽視，且可能會影響使用者的體驗。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-289">It’s also important to remember to patch network, video, USB, and audio drivers, because they’re often overlooked and can affect the user’s experience.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-290">考慮將網路、Wi-fi、影片、USB 和音訊驅動程式新增到您目前的修補程式管理程式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-290">Consider adding network, Wi-Fi, video, USB, and audio drivers to your current patch management process.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-291">我們建議您不要讓您的用戶端版本低於六個月。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-291">We recommend that you not let your client versions fall behind by more than six months.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-292">如果您使用的是 Office 隨選即用，就表示您已經隨時掌握服務的最新狀態。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-292">If you’re using Office Click-to-Run, you’re already being kept up to date by the service.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-293">使用隨附的[用戶端版本](#client-versions)（如本指南稍後所述）來協助您處理此程式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-293">Use the included [client versions](#client-versions), as described later in this guide, to assist you with this process.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-294">您也可以利用 [通話比率] 範例報告，進一步加強用戶端就緒戰略。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-294">You can also leverage the Rate My Call sample reports to further enhance your client readiness strategy.</span></span>

> [!IMPORTANT]
> <span data-ttu-id="73324-295">目前，團隊用戶端會透過 Azure 內容傳遞網路自動發佈並更新，並將由服務保持最新狀態。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-295">Currently, Teams clients are distributed and updated automatically through the Azure Content Delivery Network and will be kept up to date by the service.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-296">因此，用戶端就緒性與調查活動不適用於小組。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-296">Due to this, client readiness and investigative activities aren’t applicable to Teams.</span></span>


##### <a name="device-readiness"></a><span data-ttu-id="73324-297">裝置就緒</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-297">Device readiness</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-298">任何單一策略都不會影響使用者體驗，而不是您的裝置準備方案。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-298">No one single strategy can affect the user experience more than your device readiness strategy.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-299">大多陣列織都很樂意從使用者移除不必要的裝置（例如，手機或其他專用音訊裝置），而這通常是切換至團隊或商務用 Skype 的核心業務調整。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-299">Most organizations are happy to remove unnecessary devices (for example, desk phones or other dedicated audio devices) from users, and this is often a core business justification for switching to Teams or Skype for Business.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-300">不過，這些相同的組織有時候也能提供取代裝置，即使這些裝置成本較低也一樣。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-300">However, those same organizations sometimes hesitate to provide replacement devices, even if those devices are less expensive.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-301">使用內建麥克風和喇叭的新式膝上型電腦和電腦，不會針對商務用語音傳遞 IP （VoIP）進行優化。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-301">Modern-day laptops and PCs, though equipped with built-in microphone and speaker, aren’t optimized for business-class voice over IP (VoIP).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-302">這通常會為所有參與者產生不佳的體驗，尤其是當喇叭在嘈雜環境中時。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-302">This often creates a poor experience for all participants, especially if the speaker is in a noisy environment.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-303">Microsoft 的裝置認證計畫可確保使用者使用任何適用于團隊或商務用 Skype 認證的裝置參與電話撥打電話時，它會產生優於未認證裝置的體驗。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-303">Microsoft’s device certification program ensures that when a user participates in a phone call by using any device certified for Teams or Skype for Business, it produces an experience that’s superior to a non-certified device.</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="73324-304">我們總建議在透過桌面用戶端參與語音通話時，小組和商務用 Skype 使用者必須使用經認證的耳機或喇叭。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-304">We always recommend that Teams and Skype for Business users use a certified headset or speaker when participating in a voice call through the desktop client.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-305">如需 Microsoft 認證裝置的詳細資訊，請參閱這些有關[認證計畫](/SkypeForBusiness/certification/overview)的文章，並查看[合作夥伴解決方案目錄](https://partnersolutions.skypeforbusiness.com/solutionscatalog/personal-peripherals-pcs)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-305">For more information about Microsoft certified devices, review these articles about the [certification program](/SkypeForBusiness/certification/overview) and view the [partner solutions catalog](https://partnersolutions.skypeforbusiness.com/solutionscatalog/personal-peripherals-pcs).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-306">使用本指南稍後所述的 [[裝置] 報告](#devices)，協助您管理裝置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-306">Use the [Devices report](#devices), described later in this guide, for assistance with managing your devices.</span></span>


### <a name="categories-of-quality"></a><span data-ttu-id="73324-307">品質類別</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-307">Categories of quality</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-308">Operationalizing 高品質且可靠的部署的成功與否，取決於您的組建操作嚴格程度。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-308">The success of operationalizing a high-quality and reliable deployment depends on your building operational rigor.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-309">具體來說，請特別注意下列圖表所示的三種類別。以下是本指南的重點：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-309">Specifically, pay special attention to the three categories illustrated in the following figure; these are the focus of this guide:</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="73324-310">**網路：** 焦點在不良資料流程比率（PSR.EXE）量度、TCP 使用量、有線和無線子網上，以及識別 HTTP proxy 與 VPN 使用的音訊品質。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-310">**Network:** Audio quality focused on the Poor Stream Ratio (PSR) metric, TCP usage, wired and wireless subnets, and identifying the use of HTTP proxies and VPN.</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="73324-311">**端點：** 音訊裝置和用戶端版本（僅適用于商務用 Skype）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-311">**Endpoints:** Audio devices and client versions (Skype for Business only).</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="73324-312">**服務管理：** 此類別包含兩個區段：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-312">**Service Management:** This category comprises two sections:</span></span>

    -   <span data-ttu-id="73324-313">首先，Microsoft 必須負責管理和維護小組及商務用 Skype Online 服務。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-313">First is Microsoft’s responsibility to manage and maintain the Teams and Skype for Business Online services.</span></span>

    -   <span data-ttu-id="73324-314">第二個是貴組織必須管理的工作，以確保對服務的可靠存取，例如更新建立資訊，並在新的 Office 365 IP 位址中維護防火牆，以將基礎結構新增至服務。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-314">Second are tasks your organization must manage to ensure reliable access to the service, such as updating building information and maintaining firewalls for new Office 365 IP addresses as infrastructure is added to the service.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-315">![組織中品質類別的圖形](media/qerguide-image-categories.png "組織中的品質類別：服務管理、端點和網路。")</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-315">![Graph of the categories of quality in an organization](media/qerguide-image-categories.png "The categories of quality in an organization: service management, endpoints, and the network.")</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-316">_圖 3-小組和商務用 Skype Online 部署的重要類別_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-316">_Figure 3 - Critical categories for Teams and Skype for Business Online deployment_</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-317">下圖概要列出您必須針對每個類別執行的工作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-317">The following graphic outlines the tasks you must execute for each category.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-318">我們建議您至少一周執行這些工作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-318">We recommend that you run these tasks once a week, at a minimum.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-319">當您第一次執行這些工作時，會比後續反覆運算需要更多的精力，因為其中許多類別都需要您驗證部署設定。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-319">The first time you perform these tasks will take more effort than subsequent iterations, because many of these categories require that you validate your deployment configurations.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-320">在您達到已定義的目標之後，若要完成所需的狀態，請執行這些工作將協助您維護該狀態。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-320">After you’ve achieved the state you want by meeting the targets you’ve defined, performing these tasks will help you maintain that state.</span></span>

<!--  This is a net new graphic, never was included in the online article. OOPS! -->
<span data-ttu-id="73324-321">![每個品質類別的每週工作清單](media/qerguide-image-tasks.png "L每個品質類別的每週作業 ist ")</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-321">![List of weekly tasks per quality category](media/qerguide-image-tasks.png "List of weekly tasks per quality category")</span></span>

#### <a name="service-management-tasks"></a><span data-ttu-id="73324-322">服務管理工作</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-322">Service management tasks</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-323">在雲端-第一個世界，您必須執行特定的服務管理工作，以維持高品質的使用者體驗。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-323">In a cloud-first world, you must perform certain service management tasks to maintain high-quality user experiences.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-324">這些工作的範圍包括：確保有足夠的頻寬可達到服務，而不需要飽和網際網路連結，請確認所有受管理的網路區域的服務品質（QoS）都已就緒，且最後是在防火牆上保持在[Office 365 IP 範圍](https://aka.ms/o365ips)的最上層。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-324">These tasks range from ensuring there is sufficient bandwidth to reach the service without saturating internet links, validating that quality of service (QoS) is in place on all managed network areas, and—lastly—staying on top of [Office 365 IP ranges on firewalls](https://aka.ms/o365ips).</span></span>

#### <a name="network-tasks"></a><span data-ttu-id="73324-325">網路工作</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-325">Network tasks</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-326">網路任務有兩種類別：可靠性和品質。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-326">There are two categories of network tasks: reliability and quality.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-327">可靠性側重于測量使用者成功進行呼叫並保持連線的能力。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-327">Reliability focuses on measuring the user’s ability to make calls successfully and stay connected.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-328">[品質] 主要是在通話期間和結束後，透過使用者用戶端傳送給小組和商務用 Skype Online 的匯總遙測。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-328">Quality focuses on the aggregated telemetry sent to Teams and Skype for Business Online by the user’s client during the call and after it has ended.</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="73324-329">根據可靠性對使用者體驗的重要影響，在深入瞭解品質前，先開始評估並調查這些指標，是非常重要的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-329">Given the critical impact that reliability has on the user experience, it’s important to begin assessing and investigating those metrics before diving into quality.</span></span> 

#### <a name="endpoints-tasks"></a><span data-ttu-id="73324-330">端點任務</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-330">Endpoints tasks</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-331">此類別中的主要工作是要驗證哪些用戶端版本在過去六個月內執行桌上出版商務用 Skype，以確保使用者獲得對商務用 Skype 桌面用戶端所做的持續優化的好處。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-331">The main task in this category is validating which client versions are running Skype for Business on desktop builds from the last six months, to ensure users are getting the benefit of the continual optimizations made to the Skype for Business desktop client.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-332">此外，這簡化了整體用戶端管理工作，並提供一致的使用者體驗。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-332">Additionally, this simplifies overall client management tasks and provides a consistent user experience.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-333">另一個重要的區域就是監視您部署中流行的裝置，並推動認證裝置的使用，以提供最佳的使用者體驗。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-333">The other important area is monitoring which devices are prevalent in your deployment and driving the use of certified devices to provide the best user experience.</span></span>


> [!IMPORTANT]
> <span data-ttu-id="73324-334">目前，團隊用戶端會透過 Azure 內容傳遞網路自動發佈並更新，並將由服務保持最新狀態。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-334">Currently, Teams clients are distributed and updated automatically through the Azure Content Delivery Network and will be kept up to date by the service.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-335">用戶端準備與調查活動不適用於小組。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-335">Client readiness and investigative activities aren’t applicable to Teams.</span></span>

## <a name="cqd-basics"></a><span data-ttu-id="73324-336">CQD 基本概念</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-336">CQD basics</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-337">本節說明使用 CQD 的基本概念。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-337">This section describes the fundamentals of working with CQD.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-338">本指南是針對下列主題所提供的：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-338">Guidance is given for the following topics:</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="73324-339">什麼是 CQD？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-339">What is CQD?</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="73324-340">使用 CQD 的預期</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-340">Expectations using CQD</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="73324-341">尋找您的租使用者識別碼</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-341">Finding your tenant ID</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="73324-342">在 Microsoft 團隊與商務用 Skype 上報告</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-342">Reporting on Microsoft Teams versus Skype for Business</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="73324-343">第一和第二個分類</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-343">First versus second classifications</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="73324-344">維度、量值與篩選</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-344">Dimensions, measures, and filters</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="73324-345">資料流程與通話</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-345">Streams versus calls</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="73324-346">良好、較差及未分類通話</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-346">Good, poor, and unclassified calls</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="73324-347">常見子網</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-347">Common subnets</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-348">如需更深入的訓練和資源，請參閱[附錄](#other-resources)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-348">For more in-depth training and resources, see the [Appendix](#other-resources).</span></span>

### <a name="what-is-cqd"></a><span data-ttu-id="73324-349">什麼是 CQD？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-349">What is CQD?</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-350">您可以使用通話品質儀表板（CQD），深入瞭解使用團隊和商務用 Skype 服務所進行的通話品質。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-350">You use the Call Quality Dashboard (CQD) to gain insight into the quality of calls made by using Teams and Skype for Business services.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-351">CQD 的設計目的是協助商務用 Skype 與團隊管理員和網路工程師優化網路，並密切瞭解品質、可靠性和使用者體驗。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-351">CQD is designed to help Skype for Business and Teams admins and network engineers optimize the network and keep a close eye on quality, reliability, and the user experience.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-352">CQD 會在整個組織中查看匯總遙測，在這種情況下，整體模式可能會變得很明顯，讓員工能作出明智的評估並規劃修正活動，以最大限度地</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-352">CQD looks at aggregate telemetry for an entire organization where overall patterns can become apparent, allowing staff to make informed assessments and plan remediation activities to maximize impact.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-353">CQD 提供可讓您深入瞭解整體品質、可靠性和使用者體驗的度量報告。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-353">CQD provides reports of metrics that provide insight into overall quality, reliability, and user experience.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-354">本指南將協助您瞭解 CQD 的核心概念，以協助您在改善使用者對團隊或商務用 Skype Online 的體驗時，取得最大的影響。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-354">This guide will help in understanding the core concepts of CQD to help maximize the impact you can make in improving your users’ experience with Teams or Skype for Business Online.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-355">您可以在[附錄](#other-resources)中找到其他 CQD 資源。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-355">Additional CQD resources can be found in the [Appendix](#other-resources).</span></span>

### <a name="expectations-using-cqd"></a><span data-ttu-id="73324-356">使用 CQD 的預期</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-356">Expectations using CQD</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-357">CQD 雖然對分析趨勢和子網很有用，但並不一定會針對特定案例提供特定原因。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-357">CQD, although useful for analyzing trends and subnets, doesn’t always provide a specific cause for a given scenario.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-358">請務必瞭解這一點，並在使用 CQD 時設定正確的預期：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-358">It’s important to understand this and set the correct expectation when using CQD:</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="73324-359">CQD 不會針對每個案例提供根本原因。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-359">CQD won’t provide the root cause for every scenario.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="73324-360">CQD 不會包含電話系統或音訊會議串流。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-360">CQD won’t contain Phone System or Audio Conferencing streams.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="73324-361">CQD 將會根據趨勢來撥打進一步調查的區域。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-361">CQD will call out areas for further investigation based on trends.</span></span>

### <a name="report-editions"></a><span data-ttu-id="73324-362">報表版本</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-362">Report editions</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-363">在 CQD Online 中有兩個報表版本： [摘要] 和 [詳細]。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-363">There are two report editions in CQD Online: Summary and Detailed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-364">使用位於畫面頂端列中的下拉式功能表，開啟報表版本。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-364">Use the drop-down menu located in the bar at the top of the screen to open a report edition.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-365">所選報告版本的名稱會顯示在畫面頂端。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-365">The name of the selected report edition is displayed at the top of the screen.</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="73324-366">摘要報告是靜態報表，且無法進行編輯、下載或匯出。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-366">Summary reports are static and can’t be edited, downloaded, or exported.</span></span> 
-   <span data-ttu-id="73324-367">詳細報告可完全自訂，而且可以下載至 CSV 檔案、匯出或克隆。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-367">Detailed reports are fully customizable and can be downloaded to a CSV file, exported, or cloned.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-368">如需兩個版本之間差異的完整說明，請參閱[這篇文章](turning-on-and-using-call-quality-dashboard.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-368">For a full description of the difference between the two editions, see [this article](turning-on-and-using-call-quality-dashboard.md).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-369">_圖 4-CQD 報表類別_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-369">_Figure 4 - CQD report categories_</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-370">摘要報告分為四個類別：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-370">The summary reports are divided into four categories:</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="73324-371">**摘要報告**將重點分析品質趨勢與每日、每月和表格報告，以協助識別品質較差的子網。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-371">**Summary Reports** focus on analyzing quality trends with daily, monthly, and table reports to assist with identifying subnets that have poor quality.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-372">這是您第一次登入 CQD Online 時的預設登陸頁面。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-372">This is the default landing page when you first sign in to CQD Online.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="73324-373">**位置**改良的報告，側重于根據位置資訊來分析品質趨勢。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-373">**Location-Enhanced Reports** focus on analyzing quality trends based on location information.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-374">若要使用這些報告，您必須已上傳組建檔案。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-374">To use these reports, you must have uploaded a building file.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="73324-375">**可靠性報告**將重點放在分析音訊、影片、影片畫面共用（VBSS）和 app 共用的可靠性趨勢。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-375">**Reliability Reports** focus on analyzing reliability trends for audio, video, video-based screen sharing (VBSS), and app sharing.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="73324-376">**經驗品質報告**是一種「slimmed」的詳細 QER 範本版本，側重在分析音訊品質與可靠性的重要區域上。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-376">**Quality of Experience Reports** are a “slimmed-down” version of the detailed QER templates, focusing on key areas for analyzing audio quality and reliability.</span></span>

### <a name="report-types"></a><span data-ttu-id="73324-377">報表類型</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-377">Report types</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-378">您可以在 CQD 中選擇兩種報表類型，視您想要查看資料的方式而定。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-378">You can choose from two types of reports in CQD, depending on how you want to view your data.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-379">雖然本指南並未涵蓋在另一種類型的情況下建立一種報表類型的詳細資訊，但 QER CQD 範本提供了可自訂的圖表和表格報表，供您使用：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-379">Although this guide doesn’t cover the specifics of creating one type of report over another, the QER CQD templates provide a mix of customizable chart and table reports for you to use:</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="73324-380">[圖表報告] 建立圖形橫條圖，以視覺格式代表資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-380">Chart reports create graphical bar charts to represent data in a visual format.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-381">圖表報表最適合用於在指定的時段內視覺化資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-381">Chart reports are best used to visualize data over a given time period.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="73324-382">當您在 Microsoft Excel 中將報表匯出為 CSV 檔案以進行操作時，表格報表可用於查看個別的度量和維度。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-382">Table reports are useful for looking at individual measurements and dimensions when you export the reports to CSV files for manipulation in Microsoft Excel.</span></span>

### <a name="tenant-id"></a><span data-ttu-id="73324-383">租使用者識別碼</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-383">Tenant ID</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-384">某些 CQD 報表需要您包含租使用者識別碼的篩選器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-384">Some CQD reports require that you include a filter for your tenant ID.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-385">由於 CQD 匯總資料的方式，因此包含同盟參與者遙測。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-385">Due to the way CQD aggregates data, federated participant telemetry is included.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-386">雖然您可以在分析趨勢、用戶端和裝置報告時提供寶貴的價值，不過，您需要將資料篩選成特定租使用者，以排除同盟參與者遙測。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-386">Although this can prove valuable when analyzing trends, client and device reports require that you filter data to a specific tenant to exclude federated participant telemetry.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-387">如果您不知道您的租使用者識別碼，您可以使用下列其中一種方法來尋找它。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-387">If you don’t know your tenant ID, you can use one of the following methods to find it.</span></span>

> [!Note]
> <span data-ttu-id="73324-388">這些方法需要下列許可權：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-388">These methods require the following permissions:</span></span><ul><li><span data-ttu-id="73324-389">全域系統管理員角色</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-389">Global Administrator Role</span></span></li><li><span data-ttu-id="73324-390">商務用 Skype 系統管理員角色</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-390">Skype for Business Administrator Role</span></span></li></ul>

#### <a name="azure-portal"></a><span data-ttu-id="73324-391">Azure 入口網站</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-391">Azure portal</span></span>

1.  <span data-ttu-id="73324-392">登入 Microsoft Azure 入口網站：<https://portal.azure.com></span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-392">Sign in to the Microsoft Azure portal: <https://portal.azure.com></span></span>

2.  <span data-ttu-id="73324-393">選取 [ **Azure Active Directory**]。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-393">Select **Azure Active Directory**.</span></span>

3.  <span data-ttu-id="73324-394">在 [**管理**] 底下，選取 [**屬性**]。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-394">Under **Manage**, select **Properties**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-395">租使用者識別碼會顯示在 [**目錄識別碼**] 方塊中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-395">The tenant ID is shown in the **Directory ID** box.</span></span>

#### <a name="azure-powershell"></a><span data-ttu-id="73324-396">Azure PowerShell</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-396">Azure PowerShell</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="73324-397">[安裝 Microsoft Azure PowerShell 服務管理模組](https://docs.microsoft.com/powershell/azure/servicemanagement/install-azure-ps?view=azuresmps-4.0.0)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-397">[Install the Microsoft Azure PowerShell Service Management module](https://docs.microsoft.com/powershell/azure/servicemanagement/install-azure-ps?view=azuresmps-4.0.0).</span></span>

2. <span data-ttu-id="73324-398">出現提示時，請開啟 Azure PowerShell 命令視窗並執行下列腳本，並輸入您的 Office 365 認證：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-398">Open an Azure PowerShell command window and run the following script, entering your Office 365 credentials when prompted:</span></span> 

   ```
   Login-AzureRmAccount
   ```

3. <span data-ttu-id="73324-399">租使用者識別碼會列在輸出中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-399">The tenant ID is listed in the output.</span></span>

#### <a name="skype-for-business-online-admin-center"></a><span data-ttu-id="73324-400">商務用 Skype Online 系統管理中心</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-400">Skype for Business Online Admin Center</span></span>

1.  <span data-ttu-id="73324-401">移至<https://portal.office.com>。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-401">Go to <https://portal.office.com>.</span></span>

2.  <span data-ttu-id="73324-402">使用您的租使用者管理員組織帳戶登入。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-402">Sign in with your tenant administrator organizational account.</span></span>

3.  <span data-ttu-id="73324-403">選取 [系統**管理中心**] 底下**的 [商務用 Skype** ]。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-403">Select **Skype for Business** under **Admin Centers**.</span></span>

4.  <span data-ttu-id="73324-404">租使用者識別碼在歡迎頁面上會列為 [**組織識別碼**]。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-404">The tenant ID is listed as **Organization ID** on the Welcome page.</span></span>

#### <a name="skype-for-business-online-using-powershell"></a><span data-ttu-id="73324-405">使用 PowerShell 的商務用 Skype Online</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-405">Skype for Business Online using PowerShell</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="73324-406">[設定您的 Windows PowerShell 電腦](/SkypeForBusiness/set-up-your-computer-for-windows-powershell/set-up-your-computer-for-windows-powershell)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-406">[Set up your computer for Windows PowerShell](/SkypeForBusiness/set-up-your-computer-for-windows-powershell/set-up-your-computer-for-windows-powershell).</span></span>

2. <span data-ttu-id="73324-407">執行下列命令：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-407">Run the following command:</span></span>

   ```
   (Get-cstenant).tenantid
   ```

3. <span data-ttu-id="73324-408">租使用者識別碼會顯示為 GUID。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-408">The tenant ID is displayed as a GUID.</span></span>

### <a name="teams-vs-skype-for-business"></a><span data-ttu-id="73324-409">團隊與商務用 Skype</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-409">Teams vs. Skype for Business</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-410">CQD 可以同時報告團隊和商務用 Skype 遙測。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-410">CQD can report on both Teams and Skype for Business telemetry.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-411">不過，有時候您可能會想要開發報表來查看團隊遙測與商務用 Skype 分開的情況。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-411">However, there might be times when you want to develop a report to look at Teams telemetry separate from Skype for Business.</span></span>

#### <a name="summary-reports"></a><span data-ttu-id="73324-412">摘要報告</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-412">Summary reports</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-413">若要修改 [摘要報告] 頁面，只查看 [團隊] 或 [商務用 Skype]，請從畫面頂端選取 [**產品篩選**] 下拉式功能表，然後選取您想要的產品。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-413">To modify the summary reports page to look at only Teams or Skype for Business, select the **Product Filter** drop-down menu from the top of the screen, and then select the product you want.</span></span>

![顯示 [篩選] 選項之下拉式功能表的螢幕擷取畫面](media/qerguide-image-productfilter.png)

<span data-ttu-id="73324-415">_圖 5-選取產品篩選器_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-415">_Figure 5 - Select a Product Filter_</span></span>

#### <a name="detailed-reports"></a><span data-ttu-id="73324-416">詳細報告</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-416">Detailed reports</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-417">若要篩選所有詳細的報表，請在瀏覽器列中，將下列專案附加到 URL 的結尾：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-417">To filter all detailed reports, in the browser bar, append the following to the end of the URL:</span></span>

```
/filter/[AllStreams].[Is Teams]|[FALSE]
```

<span data-ttu-id="73324-418">**範例**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-418">**Example:**</span></span>

```https://cqd.lync.com/cqd/#/1234567/2018-5/filter/[AllStreams].[Is Teams]|[FALSE]```

<span data-ttu-id="73324-419">如需 URL 篩選的詳細資訊，請參閱本節稍後的[篩選報表](#filtering-reports)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-419">For more information about URL filters, see [Filtering reports](#filtering-reports) later in this section.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-420">若要篩選個別的詳細報表，請將``Is Teams``篩選新增至報表，並將其設定為 True 或 False。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-420">To filter an individual detailed report, add the filter ``Is Teams`` to the report and set it to True or False.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-421">如需詳細資訊，請參閱本節稍後的[編輯報表](#editing-reports)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-421">For more information, see [Editing reports](#editing-reports) later in this section.</span></span>
