<span data-ttu-id="73324-423">_圖 6-新增 Microsoft 團隊篩選至報表_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-423">_Figure 6 - Adding a Microsoft Teams filter to a report_</span></span>


### <a name="managed-vs-unmanaged-networks"></a><span data-ttu-id="73324-424">受管理的與非託管的網路</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-424">Managed vs. unmanaged networks</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-425">根據預設，CQD 中的所有端點都會分類為外部。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-425">By default, all endpoints in CQD are classified as external.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-426">一旦推出檔案，我們就可以開始查看受管理的端點資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-426">As soon as a building file is introduced, we can begin to look at managed endpoint data.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-427">如先前所述，CQD 中的網路定義為：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-427">As previously discussed, networks in CQD are defined as:</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="73324-428">_受管理的網路_（通常稱為內部或內部）會受到組織的影響及控制。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-428">A _managed network_, often referred to as internal or inside, can be influenced and controlled by the organization.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-429">這包括內部局域網、遠端 WAN 和 VPN。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-429">This includes the internal LAN, the remote WAN, and VPN.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="73324-430">_未受管理的網路_（通常稱為外部或外部）不會受到組織的影響或控制。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-430">An _unmanaged network_, often referred to as external or outside, can’t be influenced or controlled by the organization.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-431">未受管理的網路範例是賓館或機場網路。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-431">An example of an unmanaged network is a hotel or airport network.</span></span>

### <a name="dimensions-measures-and-filters"></a><span data-ttu-id="73324-432">維度、量值與篩選</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-432">Dimensions, measures, and filters</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-433">標準格式的 CQD 查詢包含下列三個參數：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-433">A well-formed CQD query contains all three of the following parameters:</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="73324-434">**維度：** 我要如何旋轉資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-434">**Dimension:** How I want to pivot on the data.</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="73324-435">**測度：** 我想要報告的內容。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-435">**Measure:** What I want to report on.</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="73324-436">**篩選：** 我要如何減少查詢所傳回的資料集。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-436">**Filter:** How I want to reduce the dataset the query returns.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-437">另一個要看的是，_維度_是分組函數，一個_量值_是我感興趣的資料，而 [_篩選_] 是我想要將結果縮小到與我的查詢相關的結果。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-437">Another way to look at this is that a _dimension_ is the grouping function, a _measure_ is the data I’m interested in, and a _filter_ is how I want to narrow down the results to those that are relevant to my query.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-438">標準格式的查詢範例會**顯示「資料流程」 [Measure] （由子網 [Dimension]）來建立 6 [Filter]**。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-438">An example of a well-formed query is **Show me Poor Streams [Measure] by Subnet [Dimension] for Building 6 [Filter]**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-439">如需詳細資訊，請參閱[CQD 中可用的維度與量值](https://aka.ms/cqd-dm)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-439">For more information, see [Dimensions and measures available in CQD](https://aka.ms/cqd-dm).</span></span>

### <a name="first-vs-second"></a><span data-ttu-id="73324-440">第一個與第二個</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-440">First vs. second</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="73324-441">CQD 中的許多維度與量值會分類為第一或第二個。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-441">Many of the dimensions and measures in CQD are classified as first or second.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-442">CQD 不使用 [來電者/被叫方] 欄位 _，因為呼叫者與被_叫方之間有中間的步驟，所以它們已_重新命名。_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-442">CQD doesn’t use caller/callee fields—these have been renamed _first_ and _second_ because there are intervening steps between the caller and callee.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-443">下列邏輯決定所涉及的端點標示為「第一」：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-443">The following logic determines which endpoint involved is labeled as first:</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="73324-444">如果是在資料流程或通話中參與伺服器，則**首先**會是伺服器端點（[會議服務器]、[中繼伺服器] 等）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-444">**First** will always be a server endpoint (Conference Server, Mediation Server, and so on) if a server is involved in the stream or call.</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="73324-445">**第二個**將一直是用戶端端點，除非資料流程位於兩個伺服器端點之間。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-445">**Second** will always be a client endpoint unless the stream is between two server endpoints.</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="73324-446">如果兩個端點都是相同類型，則首先根據使用者代理程式類別的內部順序來選擇。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-446">If both endpoints are the same type, the choice of which is first is based on internal ordering of the user agent category.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-447">這可確保順序一致。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-447">This ensures the ordering is consistent.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-448">如需判斷第一個或第二個端點相同的詳細資訊，請參閱[CQD 中可用的維度與量值](https://aka.ms/cqd-dm)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-448">For more information about determining the first or second endpoint when they’re both the same, see [Dimensions and measures available in CQD](https://aka.ms/cqd-dm).</span></span>

### <a name="stream-vs-call"></a><span data-ttu-id="73324-449">資料流程與撥號</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-449">Stream vs. call</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-450">您必須瞭解通話與資料流程間的差異，才能正確選擇您要在 CQD 中看到的維度或量值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-450">You need to understand the difference between a call and a stream to properly choose which dimensions or measures you’ll be looking at in CQD.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-451">雖然 CQD 的主要焦點是位於資料流程上，但也提供以呼叫為基礎的度量單位。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-451">Although CQD’s primary focus is on streams, call-based measurements are also available.</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="73324-452">**串流：**_資料流程_存在於兩個端點之間。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-452">**Stream:** A _stream_ exists between only two endpoints.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-453">每個方向只有一個資料流程，且需要兩個數據流才能進行通訊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-453">There is only one stream for each direction, and two streams are required for communication.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-454">資料流程對於調查建築物、網路或子網很有用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-454">Streams are useful for investigating buildings, networks, or subnets.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-455">在某些情況下，會在量化指標的名稱（例如，呼叫設定資料流程或呼叫丟棄的資料流程）中使用 call 和 stream。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-455">In some cases, both call and stream are used in the measurement’s name (for example, Call Setup Stream or Call Dropped Stream).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-456">這些專案仍會分類為串流。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-456">These are still classified as streams.</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="73324-457">**通話：**_通話_是來自所有參與者的所有資料流程的群組。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-457">**Call:** A _call_ is a grouping of all streams from all participants.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-458">通話至少包含兩個數據流。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-458">A call consists of—at minimum—two streams.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-459">單一通話至少會有兩個端點，每個端點最少為一個串流。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-459">A single call will have at least two endpoints, each with a minimum of one stream.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-460">如需有關維度或量值是參照至通話或資料流程的其他指導方針，請參閱[CQD 中可用的維度與量值](https://aka.ms/cqd-dm)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-460">For additional guidance on whether the dimension or measure is referring to a call or a stream, see [Dimensions and measures available in CQD](https://aka.ms/cqd-dm)</span></span>

### <a name="good-poor-and-unclassified-calls"></a><span data-ttu-id="73324-461">良好、較差及未分類通話</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-461">Good, poor, and unclassified calls</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-462">通話會分類為良好、較差或未分類。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-462">A call is categorized either as good, poor, or unclassified.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-463">讓我們花點時間深入討論每一個專案。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-463">Let’s take a moment to talk about each one in more detail.</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="73324-464">**良好或不佳：**[良好或較差的通話] 包含一組完整的服務度量，由服務產生並接收完整的 QoE 報告。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-464">**Good or poor:** A good or poor call consists of a call that contains a complete set of service metrics, for which a full QoE report was generated and received by the service.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-465">[在本指南前面](#poor-stream-rate)所述，判斷資料流程是否正常或較差。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-465">Determining whether a stream is good or poor is described [earlier in this guide](#poor-stream-rate).</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="73324-466">未**分類：** 未分類的資料流程不包含完整的一組服務度量單位。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-466">**Unclassified:** An unclassified stream doesn’t contain a full set of service metrics.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-467">這些可能是短通話（通常少於60秒），因為無法計算平均值，也不會產生 QoE 報告。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-467">These can be short calls—usually less than 60 seconds—where averages couldn’t be computed and a QoE report wasn’t generated.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-468">未分類呼叫最常見的原因，就是幾乎沒有資料包利用率。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-468">The most common reason for calls to be unclassified is that there was little to no packet utilization.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-469">例如，參與者在靜音和永不說話時加入會議。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-469">An example of this would be a participant who joins a meeting on mute and never speaks.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-470">參與者正在接收，但無法傳送媒體。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-470">The participant is receiving, but not transmitting, media.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-471">如果沒有傳送媒體，就不會有任何可供 CQD 用來分類端點的輸出媒體資料流程的指標。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-471">Without media being transmitted, there won’t be any metrics available for CQD to use to classify the endpoint’s outbound media stream.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-472">如需有關資料流程分類程式的詳細資訊，請參閱[這篇文章](stream-classification-in-call-quality-dashboard.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-472">For more information about the stream classification process, see [this article](stream-classification-in-call-quality-dashboard.md).</span></span>

### <a name="common-subnets"></a><span data-ttu-id="73324-473">常見子網</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-473">Common subnets</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-474">常見子網是賓館、家用網路、熱點及類似區域所使用的專用子網。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-474">Common subnets are specific private subnets that are used by hotels, home networks, hotspots, and similar areas.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-475">這些子網難以進行會審，因為其廣泛使用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-475">These subnets are difficult to triage due to their widespread use.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-476">如果您的組織使用其中一個常見的子網，我們建議您將該網路移至另一個子網。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-476">If your organization uses one of these common subnets, we recommend that you move that network to another subnet.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-477">這將使 CQD 的報告變得更容易。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-477">This will make reporting easier in CQD.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-478">請注意，[所有網路] 範本中的報告已設定為排除這些子網，以將其排除在品質較差的來源。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-478">When noted, reports in the All Networks template have been configured to exclude these subnets to eliminate them as a source of poor quality.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-479">常見的子網定義如下：其影響會因組織而異。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-479">Common subnets are defined below; their impact will vary by organization.</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="73324-480">10.0.0.0/24</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-480">10.0.0.0/24</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="73324-481">192.168.0.0/24</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-481">192.168.0.0/24</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="73324-482">192.168.1.0/24</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-482">192.168.1.0/24</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="73324-483">192.168.2.0/24</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-483">192.168.2.0/24</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="73324-484">172.20.10.0/24</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-484">172.20.10.0/24</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="73324-485">192.168.43.0/24</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-485">192.168.43.0/24</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-486">調查使用共同子網的受管理網路時，您需要使用第二個反身本機 IP 維度來組成群組子網。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-486">When investigating a managed network that uses a common subnet, you’ll need to use the Second Reflexive Local IP dimension to group subnets.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-487">此維度包含端點的公用 IP 位址。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-487">This dimension contains the endpoint’s public IP address.</span></span>

## <a name="cqd-online"></a><span data-ttu-id="73324-488">線上 CQD</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-488">CQD Online</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-489">本節說明存取 CQD 的基本概念。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-489">This section describes the fundamentals of accessing CQD.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-490">本指南是針對下列主題所提供的：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-490">Guidance is given for the following topics:</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="73324-491">線上存取 CQD</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-491">Accessing CQD online</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="73324-492">CQD 快速入門</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-492">Getting started with CQD</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="73324-493">在 CQD 中編輯報表</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-493">Editing reports in CQD</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="73324-494">篩選 CQD 中的報表</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-494">Filtering reports in CQD</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="73324-495">在 CQD 中匯入報表</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-495">Importing reports in CQD</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-496">如需更深入的訓練和資源，請參閱[附錄](#other-resources)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-496">For more in-depth training and resources, see the [Appendix](#other-resources).</span></span>

### <a name="access-cqd-online"></a><span data-ttu-id="73324-497">線上存取 CQD</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-497">Access CQD Online</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-498">您可以透過下列三種方式之一來存取 CQD：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-498">You can access CQD one of three ways:</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="73324-499">移至<https://cqd.lync.com>。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-499">Go to <https://cqd.lync.com>.</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="73324-500">移至 [ **Microsoft 團隊系統管理中心**]，然後選取要 CQD 的連結，如下圖所示。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-500">Go to **Microsoft Teams admin center** and select the link to CQD, as shown in the following illustration.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-507">當您第一次流覽至 CQD 時，您會看到 [摘要報告] 頁面。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-507">When you first browse to CQD, you’ll see the Summary Reports page.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-508">本指南中所述的大部分報告都是自訂的詳細報告。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-508">Most of the reports described in this guide are custom detailed reports.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-509">若要開始使用詳細報表，請選取頁面頂端的 [**摘要報表**]，然後選擇 [**詳細報表**]。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-509">To get started using the detailed reports, select **Summary Reports** at the top of the page, and then choose **Detailed Reports**.</span></span>

### <a name="editing-reports"></a><span data-ttu-id="73324-526">編輯報表</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-526">Editing reports</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-527">當您在報表的 [動作] 功能表上選取 [**編輯**] 時，會開啟 [查詢編輯器]。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-527">When you select **Edit** on the action menu of a report, you’ll open Query Editor.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-528">每個報告都受 CQD 查詢的支援。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-528">Each report is backed by a query to CQD.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-529">報表是其查詢所傳回資料的視覺效果。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-529">A report is a visualization of the data returned by its query.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-530">[查詢編輯器] 是一個 UI，除了報表的顯示選項之外，還能編輯這些查詢，如下圖所示。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-530">The Query Editor is a UI for editing these queries in addition to the display options for the report, as illustrated in the following figure.</span></span>

### <a name="filtering-reports"></a><span data-ttu-id="73324-546">篩選報表</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-546">Filtering reports</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-547">提供的範本包括數個內建查詢和報表篩選。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-547">The templates provided include several built-in queries and report filters.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-548">下列各節說明在整個範本中使用的最常見篩選。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-548">The following sections describe the most common filters used throughout the templates.</span></span>

#### <a name="url-filter"></a><span data-ttu-id="73324-549">URL 篩選</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-549">URL filter</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-550">您可以使用 URL 篩選來篩選特定維度的每個報表。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-550">You can use a URL filter to filter every report for a specific dimension.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-551">最常見的 URL 篩選是用來篩選報告，以排除同盟參與者遙測，或將焦點放在團隊或商務用 Skype Online 上。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-551">The most common URL filters are used to filter reports to exclude federated participant telemetry, or focus on Teams or Skype for Business Online.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-552">我們建議您在使用篩選時，為它們加上書簽，以方便參考。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-552">We recommend that when using filters, you bookmark them for easy reference.</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="73324-553">如果您要修正受管理的建築物或網路（其中的同盟端點可能會影響您的報表），則從 CQD 報告排除同盟資料就很有用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-553">Excluding federated data from CQD reports is useful when you’re remediating managed buildings or networks where federated endpoints might influence your reports.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-554">若要實現 URL 篩選，請在瀏覽器位址列中，將下列專案附加到 URL 的結尾：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-554">To implement a URL filter, in the browser address bar, append the following to the end of the URL:</span></span>

```
/filter/[AllStreams].[Second Tenant Id]\|[YOUR TENANT ID HERE]
```

<span data-ttu-id="73324-555">範例</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-555">Example:</span></span>  

```https://cqd.lync.com/cqd/#/1234567/2018-08/filter/[AllStreams].[Second Tenant Id]|[TENANTID]```

<span data-ttu-id="73324-556">若要篩選團隊或商務用 Skype 的報表，請將下列專案附加到 URL 的結尾：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-556">To filter the reports for Teams or Skype for Business, append the following to the end of the URL:</span></span>

```
/filter/[AllStreams].[Is Teams]|[TRUE | FALSE]
```

<span data-ttu-id="73324-557">範例</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-557">Example:</span></span>

```https://cqd.lync.com/cqd/#/1234567/2018-08/filter/[AllStreams].[Is Teams]|[TRUE]```


> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="73324-558">上述 URL 範例只適用于視覺標記法。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-558">The URL examples above are for visual representation only.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-559">請使用預設的 CQD 連結<https://cqd.lync.com>。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-559">Please use the default CQD link of <https://cqd.lync.com>.</span></span>


#### <a name="query-filters"></a><span data-ttu-id="73324-560">查詢篩選</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-560">Query filters</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-561">查詢篩選是透過使用 CQD 中的 [查詢編輯器] 來實現。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-561">Query filters are implemented by using the Query Editor in CQD.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-562">這些篩選可用來減少 CQD 傳回的記錄數，從而將報表的整體大小和查詢時間降至最低。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-562">These filters are used to reduce the number of records returned by CQD, thus minimizing the report’s overall size and query times.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-563">這對於篩選掉未受管理的網路特別有用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-563">This is especially useful for filtering out unmanaged networks.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-564">下表所列的篩選使用正則運算式（RegEx）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-564">The filters listed in the following table use regular expressions (RegEx).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-565">_表格 3-查詢篩選_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-565">_Table 3 - Query filters_</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="73324-566">Filter</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-566">Filter</span></span>         | <span data-ttu-id="73324-567">描述</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-567">Description</span></span>          | <span data-ttu-id="73324-568">CQD 查詢篩選範例</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-568">CQD query filter example</span></span>      |
|----------------|----------------------|-------------------------------|
| <span data-ttu-id="73324-569">沒有空白值</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-569">No blank values</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="73324-570">有些篩選沒有選項可篩選空白值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-570">Some filters don’t have the option to filter for blank values.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-571">若要手動篩選空白值，請根據您的需求，使用空白運算式，並將篩選設定為 [等於] 或 [不等於]。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-571">To filter blank values manually, use the blank expression and set the filter to Equals or Not Equals, depending on your needs.</span></span>      | <span data-ttu-id="73324-572">第二個\< \> \^ \\建築物名稱 s\*\$</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-572">Second Building Name \<\> \^\\s\*\$</span></span>                       |
| <span data-ttu-id="73324-573">排除常見子網</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-573">Exclude common subnets</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="73324-574">若沒有有效的組建檔案，無法從非託管網路個別管理，就會將 [家用網路] 包含在報告中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-574">Without a valid building file to separate managed from unmanaged networks, home networks will be included in the reports.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-575">這些 home 子網不在其控制範圍內，而且可以從報表中快速排除。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-575">These home subnets are outside the scope of IT’s control and can be quickly excluded from a report.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-576">在本指南中定義的常見子網是10.0.0.0、192.168.1.0 和192.168.0.0。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-576">Common subnets, as defined in this guide, are 10.0.0.0, 192.168.1.0 and 192.168.0.0.</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="73324-577">第二\< \>個子\|網\| 10.0.0.0 192.168.0.0 192.168.1。0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-577">Second Subnet \<\> 10.0.0.0 \| 192.168.0.0 \| 192.168.1.0</span></span> |
| <span data-ttu-id="73324-578">僅限內部查看</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-578">View inside only</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="73324-579">用來篩選受管理（內部）或非託管（外部）的報表。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-579">Used to filter a report for managed (inside) or unmanaged (outside).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-580">受管理的 CQD 範本已預先設定了這些篩選器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-580">The managed CQD template is already preconfigured with these filters.</span></span>       | <span data-ttu-id="73324-581">Corp = 內部的秒數</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-581">Second Inside Corp = Inside</span></span>        |

#### <a name="report-filters"></a><span data-ttu-id="73324-582">報表篩選</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-582">Report filters</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-583">您可以透過在 [查詢編輯器] 或直接在報表中新增篩選，來實現報表篩選。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-583">Report filters are implemented by adding a filter to the rendered report either in the Query Editor or directly to the report.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-584">下列報表篩選是在整個範本中使用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-584">The following report filters are used throughout the template.</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="73324-586">Filter</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-586">Filter</span></span>     | <span data-ttu-id="73324-587">描述</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-587">Description</span></span>                            | <span data-ttu-id="73324-588">CQD 報表篩選範例</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-588">CQD report filter example</span></span>         |
|------------|----------------------------------------|-----------------------------------|
| <span data-ttu-id="73324-589">月</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-589">Month</span></span>      | <span data-ttu-id="73324-590">首先從年份開始，然後從月份開始。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-590">Start with the year first, then month.</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="73324-591">2017-10</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-591">2017-10</span></span>                           |

## <a name="import-the-cqd-templates"></a><span data-ttu-id="73324-601">匯入 CQD 範本</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-601">Import the CQD templates</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-602">本指南包含[兩個策劃 CQD 範本](https://aka.ms/qertemplates)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-602">This guide includes [two curated CQD templates](https://aka.ms/qertemplates).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-603">這些範本可提高 CQD 的使用速度，並提供您快速利用 CQD 功能來影響使用者團隊或商務用 Skype 體驗的機會。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-603">These templates accelerate your usage of CQD and provide you an opportunity to quickly leverage CQD’s capabilities to make an impact on your users’ Teams or Skype for Business experience.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-604">[所有網路] 範本（雖然經過優化，可搭配建立資料檔案使用），但您可以在向 CQD 中進行收集及上傳資訊時使用，如下一節所述。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-604">The All Networks template, though optimized to work with a building data file, can be used while you work toward collecting and uploading building information into CQD, as described in the next section.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-605">**若要匯入範本（。CQDX）進入 CQD Online**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-605">**To import the templates (.CQDX) into CQD Online**</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="73324-606">移至<https://cqd.lync.com>。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-606">Go to <https://cqd.lync.com>.</span></span>

2. <span data-ttu-id="73324-607">使用您的 Office 365 系統管理認證進行驗證。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-607">Authenticate by using your Office 365 Administrative credentials.</span></span>

   > [!NOTE]
   > <span data-ttu-id="73324-608">您必須具備 Office 365 全域系統管理員、商務用 Skype 系統管理員或報表閱讀者角色，才能存取 CQD。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-608">You must have the Office 365 Global Administrator, Skype for Business Administrator, or Report Readers role to access CQD.</span></span> 

3. <span data-ttu-id="73324-609">選取頁面頂端的 [**摘要報表**] 功能表，然後選擇 [**詳細報表**]。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-609">Select the **Summary Reports** menu at the top of the page, and then choose **Detailed Reports**.</span></span>

4. <span data-ttu-id="73324-610">在 [摘要] 窗格中，選取 [匯**入**]。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-610">On the summary pane, select **Import**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-611">移至 CQDX 已儲存的位置，選取 [CQDX] 範本，然後選取 [**開啟**]。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-611">Go to the CQDX saved location, select the CQDX template, and then select **Open**.</span></span>

5. <span data-ttu-id="73324-612">在上傳範本之後，會出現一個快顯視窗，顯示「已成功匯入報告」訊息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-612">After the template is uploaded, a pop-up window will display the message “Report import was successful.”</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-613">選取 **[確定]。**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-613">Select **OK.**</span></span>

   <span data-ttu-id="73324-614">![成功匯入通知的螢幕擷取畫面](media/qerguide-image-importmessage.png "已成功匯入範本的通知")</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-614">![Screen shot of successful import notification](media/qerguide-image-importmessage.png "Notification that the template was successfully imported")</span></span>

6. <span data-ttu-id="73324-615">針對第二個 CQD 範本重複步驟4和5。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-615">Repeat steps 4 and 5 for the second CQD template.</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="73324-616">CQD 範本是針對每位使用者匯入。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-616">The CQD templates are imported per user.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-617">如果其他使用者需要使用報告，他們必須登入範本，並將其匯入其 CQD 實例。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-617">If additional users need to use the report, they must sign in and import the templates into their CQD instance.</span></span> 


## <a name="building-mapping"></a><span data-ttu-id="73324-618">建立對應</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-618">Building mapping</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-619">在團隊或商務用 Skype Online 部署中，所有用戶端都是外部的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-619">In a Teams or Skype for Business Online deployment, all clients are external.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-620">也就是說，根據預設，所有用戶端都會在 CQD Online 中報告為外部，不論用戶端是否已連線到內部公司網路。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-620">That has the implication that by default, all clients are reported as outside in CQD Online, regardless of whether the client was connected on an internal corporate network.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-621">當您使用 CQD 時，您必須知道端點的位置，以及它是否已連線至您可以管理的網路，或是您無法管理的網路（假設您只能改善可管理的網路）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-621">When you work with CQD, you need to know the location of an endpoint and whether it was connected to a network you can manage or a network you can’t manage—the assumption being that you can only improve networks you can manage.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-622">透過將子網和組建資訊上傳到 CQD Online，您就能讓 CQD 判斷端點是否已連線至內部的公司/受管理網路或外部/非託管網路。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-622">By uploading subnet and building information to CQD Online, you enable CQD to determine whether the endpoint was connected to an internal corporate/managed network or to an external/unmanaged network.</span></span>

### <a name="building-data-file-structure"></a><span data-ttu-id="73324-623">建立資料檔案結構</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-623">Building data file structure</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-624">您上傳的資料檔格式必須符合下列需求，才能在上傳前通過驗證檢查。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-624">The format of the data file you upload must meet the following requirements to pass the validation check before uploading.</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="73324-625">檔案必須是 TSV 檔案，這表示每個資料列都是以 Tab 字元分隔，或是以逗號分隔每個資料行的 CSV 檔案。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-625">The file must be either a TSV file—which means that for each row, each column is separated by a Tab character—or a CSV file in which each column is separated by a comma.</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="73324-626">檔案不能大於 50 MB。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-626">The file can’t be larger than 50 MB.</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="73324-627">資料檔案的內容*不能包含表格標題*。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-627">The content of the data file *must not include table headers*.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-628">換句話說，資料檔案的第一行必須是實際資料，而不是欄標題（例如 "Network"）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-628">In other words, the first line of the data file must be real data, not column headings such as “Network.”</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="73324-629">針對每個資料行，資料類型只能是 String、Number 或 Bool。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-629">For each column, the data type can only be String, Number, or Bool.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-630">如果資料類型是 Number，則該值必須是一個數值;如果是 Bool，則該值必須是0或1。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-630">If the data type is Number, the value must be a numeric value; if it’s Bool, the value must be either 0 or 1.</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="73324-631">針對每個資料行，如果資料類型是 String，則資料可以是空白（但必須以適當的分隔符號分隔，也就是 Tab 字元或逗號）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-631">For each column, if the data type is String, the data can be empty (but still must be separated by an appropriate delimiter—that is, a Tab character or comma).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-632">這只會將該欄位指派為空白字串值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-632">This just assigns that field an empty string value.</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="73324-633">每個資料列都必須有14個數據行。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-633">There must be 14 columns for each row.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-634">每一欄都必須具有下表所述的資料類型，而且這些欄必須按照資料表中所列的順序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-634">Each column must have the data type described in the following table, and the columns must be in the order listed in the table.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-635">_表 5-建立檔結構_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-635">_Table 5 - Building file structure_</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="73324-636">欄名稱</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-636">Column name</span></span>        | <span data-ttu-id="73324-637">資料類型</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-637">Data type</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="73324-638">範例</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-638">Example</span></span>                   | <span data-ttu-id="73324-639">級</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-639">Guidance</span></span>    |
|--------------------|-----------|---------------------------|-------------|
| <span data-ttu-id="73324-640">網路</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-640">Network</span></span>            | <span data-ttu-id="73324-641">String</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-641">String</span></span>    | <span data-ttu-id="73324-642">192.168.1.0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-642">192.168.1.0</span></span>               | <span data-ttu-id="73324-643">必要</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-643">Required</span></span>    |
| <span data-ttu-id="73324-644">NetworkName</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-644">NetworkName</span></span>        | <span data-ttu-id="73324-645">String</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-645">String</span></span>    | <span data-ttu-id="73324-646">美國/西雅圖/西雅圖-海-1</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-646">USA/Seattle/SEATTLE-SEA-1</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="73324-647">必要\*</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-647">Required\*</span></span>  |

| <span data-ttu-id="73324-652">BuildingName</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-652">BuildingName</span></span>       | <span data-ttu-id="73324-653">String</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-653">String</span></span>    | <span data-ttu-id="73324-654">北京-海-1</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-654">SEATTLE-SEA-1</span></span>             | <span data-ttu-id="73324-655">必要\*</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-655">Required\*</span></span>  |
| <span data-ttu-id="73324-656">OwnershipType</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-656">OwnershipType</span></span>      | <span data-ttu-id="73324-657">String</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-657">String</span></span>    | <span data-ttu-id="73324-658">尚未</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-658">Contoso</span></span>                   | <span data-ttu-id="73324-659">選用</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-659">Optional</span></span>    |
| <span data-ttu-id="73324-660">BuildingType</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-660">BuildingType</span></span>       | <span data-ttu-id="73324-661">String</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-661">String</span></span>    | <span data-ttu-id="73324-662">終止</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-662">IT Termination</span></span>            | <span data-ttu-id="73324-663">選用</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-663">Optional</span></span>    |

| <span data-ttu-id="73324-672">郵遞區號</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-672">ZipCode</span></span>            | <span data-ttu-id="73324-673">String</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-673">String</span></span>    | <span data-ttu-id="73324-674">98001</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-674">98001</span></span>                     | <span data-ttu-id="73324-675">採用</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-675">Recommended</span></span> |
| <span data-ttu-id="73324-676">國家</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-676">Country</span></span>            | <span data-ttu-id="73324-677">String</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-677">String</span></span>    | <span data-ttu-id="73324-678">一下</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-678">US</span></span>                        | <span data-ttu-id="73324-679">採用</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-679">Recommended</span></span> |
| <span data-ttu-id="73324-680">市</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-680">State</span></span>              | <span data-ttu-id="73324-681">String</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-681">String</span></span>    | <span data-ttu-id="73324-682">華盛頓</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-682">WA</span></span>                        | <span data-ttu-id="73324-683">採用</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-683">Recommended</span></span> |
| <span data-ttu-id="73324-684">地區</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-684">Region</span></span>             | <span data-ttu-id="73324-685">String</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-685">String</span></span>    | <span data-ttu-id="73324-686">MSUS</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-686">MSUS</span></span>                      | <span data-ttu-id="73324-687">採用</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-687">Recommended</span></span> |
| <span data-ttu-id="73324-688">InsideCorp</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-688">InsideCorp</span></span>         | <span data-ttu-id="73324-689">Bool</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-689">Bool</span></span>      | <span data-ttu-id="73324-690">1</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-690">1</span></span>                         | <span data-ttu-id="73324-691">必要</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-691">Required</span></span>    |
| <span data-ttu-id="73324-692">ExpressRoute</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-692">ExpressRoute</span></span>       | <span data-ttu-id="73324-693">Bool</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-693">Bool</span></span>      | <span data-ttu-id="73324-694">0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-694">0</span></span>                         | <span data-ttu-id="73324-695">必要</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-695">Required</span></span>    |

<span data-ttu-id="73324-696">\*CQD 不需要時，範本會設定為顯示建築物和網路名稱。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-696">\*While not required by CQD, the templates are configured to display Building and Network name.</span></span>

#### <a name="supernetting"></a><span data-ttu-id="73324-697">Supernetting</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-697">Supernetting</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-698">您可以使用 supernetting （通常稱為無類別的網域間路由（CIDR））來取代定義每個子網。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-698">You can use supernetting, commonly called Classless Inter-Domain Routing (CIDR,) in place of defining each subnet.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-699">*Supernet*是多個子網的組合，可共用單一路由前置詞。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-699">A *supernet* is a combination of several subnets that share a single routing prefix.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-700">您可以使用 supernetted 位址，而不是為每個子網新增專案。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-700">Instead of adding an entry for each subnet, you can use the supernetted address.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-701">支援 Supernetting，但我們不建議使用它。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-701">Supernetting is supported, but we don’t recommend using it.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-702">例如，Contoso 的行銷大樓是由下列子網組成：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-702">For example, Contoso’s marketing building is made up of the subnets below:</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="73324-703">10.1.0.0/24-第一層</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-703">10.1.0.0/24—first floor</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="73324-704">10.1.1.0/24-第二層</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-704">10.1.1.0/24—second floor</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="73324-705">10.1.2.0/24-第三層</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-705">10.1.2.0/24—third floor</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="73324-706">10.1.3.0/24-第四層</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-706">10.1.3.0/24—fourth floor</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-707">您可以使用 supernetted 位址（在此範例中為 10.1.0.0/22），而不是為每個子網上新增專案。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-707">Instead of adding an entry for each subnet, you can use the supernetted address—in this example, 10.1.0.0/22.</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="73324-708">Network = 10.1.0。0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-708">Network = 10.1.0.0</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="73324-709">網路範圍 = 22</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-709">Network Range = 22</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-710">在執行 supernetting 之前，請先考慮以下幾點：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-710">Here are a few things to consider before you implement supernetting:</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="73324-711">Supernetting 只能在含有8位到28位元遮罩的子網對應中使用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-711">Supernetting can only be used in a subnet mapping with 8-bit to 28-bit mask.</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="73324-712">Supernetting 佔用較少的時間，但代價是減少資料的豐富程度。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-712">Supernetting takes less time up front, but it comes at the cost of reducing the richness of your data.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-713">假設有一個涉及子網200.1.2.0 的品質問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-713">Let’s say there’s a quality problem involving subnet 200.1.2.0.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-714">如果您已執行 supernetting，就不會知道子網的組建位置或網路類型（例如，lab）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-714">If you implemented supernetting, you won’t know where in the building the subnet is located or what type of network it is (for example, a lab).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-715">如果您已定義所有子網，以取得建築物和上傳的樓層位置資訊，您就可以看到這種差異。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-715">If you’d defined all the subnets for a building and uploaded floor location information, you’d be able to see that distinction.</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="73324-716">務必確保 supernetted 位址正確無誤，而且不會捕捉不想要的子網。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-716">It’s important to ensure that the supernetted address is correct and isn’t catching unwanted subnets.</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="73324-717">在資料中找到192.168.0.0 是很常見的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-717">It’s quite common to find 192.168.0.0 in data.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-718">對於許多組織而言，這表示使用者是在家中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-718">For many organizations, this indicates that the user is at home.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-719">對其他人而言，這是衛星辦公室的 IP 位址配置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-719">For others, this is the IP address scheme for a satellite office.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-720">如果您的組織有使用這項設定的辦事處，請不要將它納入您的組建檔案中，因為很難使用通用子網來區分家用和內部網路。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-720">If your organization does have offices that use this configuration, don’t include it in your building file because it’s difficult to distinguish between home and internal networks by using common subnets.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-721">請參閱本指南前面的有關[常見子網](#common-subnets)的章節。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-721">See the section about [common subnets](#common-subnets), earlier in this guide.</span></span>

> [!IMPORTANT]
> <span data-ttu-id="73324-722">網路範圍可以用來代表 supernet。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-722">The network range can be used to represent a supernet.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-723">所有新的組建資料檔案上傳都將會檢查任何重迭的範圍。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-723">All new building data file uploads will be checked for any overlapping ranges.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-724">如果您先前上傳的是組建檔案，您應該下載目前的檔案並再次上傳，以找出任何重迭並修正問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-724">If you’ve previously uploaded a building file, you should download the current file and upload it again to identify any overlaps and fix the issue.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-725">先前上傳的檔案中的任何交疊，可能會導致無法正確地將子網對應至報表中的建築物。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-725">Any overlap in previously uploaded files might result in the wrong mappings of subnets to buildings in the reports.</span></span>

#### <a name="vpn"></a><span data-ttu-id="73324-726">點對點</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-726">VPN</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-727">用戶端傳送至 Office 365 的體驗品質（QoE）資料（也就是 CQD 資料來源的位置），包括 VPN 標誌。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-727">The quality of experience (QoE) data that clients send to Office 365—which is where CQD data is sourced from—includes a VPN flag.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-728">CQD 將會看到此為第一個 VPN 和第二個 VPN 維度。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-728">CQD will see this as the First VPN and Second VPN dimensions.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-729">不過，此標記會依賴 VPN 廠商的報告來向 Windows 確認 VPN 網路介面卡已註冊為遠端存取配接器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-729">However, this flag relies on VPN vendors’ reporting to Windows that the VPN network adapter registered is a Remote Access adapter.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-730">並非所有的 VPN 供應商都正確註冊遠端存取配接器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-730">Not all VPN vendors properly register Remote Access adapters.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-731">因此，您可能無法使用內建的 VPN 查詢篩選。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-731">Because of this, you might not be able to use the built-in VPN query filters.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-732">在建立資訊檔案中，有兩種方法可容納 VPN 子網：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-732">There are two approaches to accommodating VPN subnets in the building information file:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="73324-733">在此欄位中使用 VPN 子網的文字「VPN」來定義**網路名稱**。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-733">Define a **Network Name** by using the text “VPN” in this field for VPN subnets.</span></span>

  ![使用網路名稱顯示 VPN 的 QCD 報告螢幕擷取畫面](media/qerguide-image-vpnnetworkname.png)

  <span data-ttu-id="73324-735">_圖 12-使用網路名稱的 VPN_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-735">_Figure 12 - VPN using network name_</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="73324-736">在此欄位中使用 VPN 子網的文字「VPN」來定義**建築物名稱**。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-736">Define a **Building Name** by using the text “VPN” in this field for VPN subnets.</span></span>

  ![使用建築物名稱顯示 VPN 的 QCD 報告螢幕擷取畫面](media/qerguide-image-vpnbuildingname.png)

  <span data-ttu-id="73324-738">_圖 13-使用建築物名稱的 VPN_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-738">_Figure 13 - VPN using building name_</span></span>

> [!IMPORTANT]
> <span data-ttu-id="73324-739">某些 VPN 實現不會精確地報告子網資訊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-739">Certain VPN implementations don’t accurately report subnet information.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-740">如果您在報表中出現這種情況，建議您將 VPN 子網新增至組建檔案，而不是子網的一個專案，就會將 VPN 子網上每個位址的個別專案新增成獨立的32位網路。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-740">If this occurs in your reporting, we recommend that when you add a VPN subnet to the building file, instead of one entry for the subnet, add separate entries for each address in the VPN subnet as a separate 32-bit network.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-741">每個資料列都可以有相同的建築物中繼資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-741">Each row can have the same building metadata.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-742">例如，如果 172.16.18.0/24 不是一列，則會有253列，每個位址都有一個列，其中每個位址都是從 172.16.18.1/32 至 172.16.18.254/32 （含）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-742">For example, instead of one row for 172.16.18.0/24, you have 253 rows, with one row for each address from 172.16.18.1/32 through 172.16.18.254/32, inclusive.</span></span>


> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="73324-743">已已知 VPN 連線在基礎網際網路連線為無線時，將網路連線 misidentify 為有線。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-743">VPN connections have been known to misidentify the network connection as wired when the underlying internet connection is wireless.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-744">當您以 VPN 連線查看品質時，您無法假設正確識別了連線類型。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-744">When looking at quality over VPN connections, you can’t assume that the connection type has been accurately identified.</span></span>

### <a name="uploading-building-information"></a><span data-ttu-id="73324-745">上傳建築物資訊</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-745">Uploading building information</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-746">CQD 摘要報告儀表板包含租使用者的**資料上傳**頁面，可透過選取右上角的 [**租使用者資料上傳**連結] 標記來存取（尋找齒輪圖示）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-746">The CQD Summary Reports dashboard includes a **Tenant Data Upload** page, accessed by selecting the **Tenant Data Upload** link tag in the upper-right corner (look for the gear icon).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-747">此頁面可供系統管理員上傳自己的資訊，例如 IP 位址和地理資訊的對應、對應每個無線存取點及其 MAC 位址等。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-747">This page is used for admins to upload their own information, such as mapping of IP address and geographical information, mapping each wireless access point and its MAC address, and so on.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="73324-748">流覽至以<https://cqd.lync.com>線上前往 CQD。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-748">Go to CQD Online by browsing to <https://cqd.lync.com>.</span></span>

2. <span data-ttu-id="73324-749">選取右上角的齒輪圖示，然後從 [**摘要報告**] 頁面選擇 [**租使用者資料上傳**]。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-749">Select the gear icon in the upper-right corner, and choose **Tenant Data Upload** from the **Summary Reports** page.</span></span>

   ![上傳資料時出現的對話方塊螢幕擷取畫面](media/qerguide-image-tenantdataupload.png)

   <span data-ttu-id="73324-751">_圖 14-租使用者資料上傳功能表_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-751">_Figure 14 - Tenant Data Upload menu_</span></span>

3. <span data-ttu-id="73324-752">或者，如果這是您第一次造訪 CQD，系統會要求您上傳 [組建資料]。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-752">Alternatively, if this is your first time visiting CQD, you’ll be asked to upload building data.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-753">您可以選取 **[立即上傳**]，快速流覽至 [**租使用者資料上傳**] 頁面。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-753">You can select **Upload Now** to quickly navigate to the **Tenant Data Upload** page.</span></span>

   ![通知使用者上傳建立資料的橫幅螢幕擷取畫面](media/qerguide-image-buildingdatauploadbanner.png)

   <span data-ttu-id="73324-755">_圖 15-建立資料上傳橫幅_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-755">_Figure 15 - Building data upload banner_</span></span>

4. <span data-ttu-id="73324-756">在 [**租使用者資料上傳**] 頁面上，選取 **[流覽]** 來選擇資料檔案。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-756">On the **Tenant Data Upload** page, select **Browse** to choose a data file.</span></span>

5. <span data-ttu-id="73324-757">選取資料檔之後，請指定**開始日期**，也可以指定結束日期。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-757">After selecting a data file, specify **Start date** and, optionally, specify an end date.</span></span>

6. <span data-ttu-id="73324-758">選取 [**開始日期**] 後，選取 **[上傳**]，將檔案上傳到 CQD。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-758">After selecting **Start date**, select **Upload** to upload the file to CQD.</span></span> <br><br><span data-ttu-id="73324-759">檔案上傳之前，會進行驗證。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-759">Before the file is uploaded, it’s validated.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-760">如果驗證失敗，則會顯示一則錯誤訊息，要求您更正檔案。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-760">If validation fails, an error message is displayed requesting that you correct the file.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-761">下圖顯示當資料檔案中的欄數不正確時所發生的錯誤。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-761">The following figure shows an error occurring when the number of columns in the data file is incorrect.</span></span>

   ![顯示組建資料上傳錯誤的對話方塊範例](media/qerguide-image-buildingdatauploaderror.png)
 
   <span data-ttu-id="73324-763">_圖 16-建立資料上傳錯誤_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-763">_Figure 16 - Building data upload error_</span></span>

7. <span data-ttu-id="73324-764">如果驗證期間沒有發生任何錯誤，檔案上傳就會成功。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-764">If no errors occur during validation, the file upload will succeed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-765">接著，您可以在 [我的上**傳**] 資料表中看到上傳的資料檔，該檔案會在該頁面的底部顯示目前租使用者的所有已上傳檔案的完整清單。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-765">You can then see the uploaded data file in the **My uploads** table, which shows the full list of all uploaded files for the current tenant at the bottom of that page.</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="73324-766">可能需要長達四個小時的時間，才能完成建立檔的處理。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-766">It can take up to four hours to finish processing the building file.</span></span> <br><br> <span data-ttu-id="73324-767">如果您已上傳檔案，且需要新增可能已錯過或排除的子網，請修改原始檔案，方法是新增子網、移除目前的檔案，然後重新上傳新編輯的檔案。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-767">If you’ve already uploaded a building file and need to add subnets that might have been missed or excluded, modify the original file by adding the new subnets, remove the current file, and re-upload the newly edited file.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-768">在 CQD 中，只能有一個作用中的組建資料檔案。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-768">There can be only one active building data file in CQD.</span></span> 


### <a name="updating-a-building-file"></a><span data-ttu-id="73324-769">更新組建檔案</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-769">Updating a building file</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-770">在收集建立和子網資訊時，系統管理員會經常在一段時間內，在多個反覆運算中上傳檔案，並在新的子網變為可用時，新增其建築物資訊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-770">While gathering building and subnet information, administrators will often upload the building file in multiple iterations over time, adding new subnets and their building information as it becomes available.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-771">發生這種情況時，您必須重新上傳您的組建檔案。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-771">When this occurs, you’ll need to re-upload your building file.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-772">此程式就像上一節所述的初始上傳一樣，還有一些例外狀況，如下一節所述。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-772">This process is like the initial upload as described in the previous section, with a few exceptions as noted in the following section.</span></span>

> [!Important]
> <span data-ttu-id="73324-773">一次只能有一個建立檔。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-773">Only one building file can be active at a time.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-774">多個建築物檔案不是累加的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-774">Multiple building files aren’t cumulative.</span></span>

#### <a name="adding-net-new-subnets"></a><span data-ttu-id="73324-775">新增全新子網</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-775">Adding net new subnets</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-776">在某些情況下，您需要將全新的子網新增至 CQD，而不是原本是您的網路拓朴的一部分。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-776">There are times when you’ll need to add net new subnets to CQD that weren’t originally part of your network topology.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-777">若要新增 net 新建子網，請在 CQD 租使用者資料上傳入口網站中執行下列動作：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-777">To add net new subnets, do the following in the CQD Tenant Data Upload portal:</span></span>

1.  <span data-ttu-id="73324-778">編輯原始的組建檔案，並提供至少在取得網路新子網前一天的結束日期。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-778">Edit the original building file and provide an end date that occurs at least one day before the net new subnets were acquired.</span></span>
2.  <span data-ttu-id="73324-779">如果您還沒有最新的複本，請下載原始檔案。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-779">Download the original file, if you don’t already have an up-to-date copy.</span></span>
3.  <span data-ttu-id="73324-780">將全新的子網附加至原始的組建檔案。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-780">Append the net new subnets to the original building file.</span></span>
4.  <span data-ttu-id="73324-781">按照上述相同程式上傳新修改的組建檔案，並在前一個建築物檔案結束後，將 [開始日期] 設定為一天。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-781">Upload the newly modified building file following the same process as above, and set the start date for one day after the previous building file ends.</span></span>

#### <a name="updating-the-current-building-file"></a><span data-ttu-id="73324-782">更新目前的組建檔案</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-782">Updating the current building file</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-783">如果已上傳檔案，但是您需要新增遺失的子網，請在 CQD 租使用者資料上傳入口網站中執行下列動作：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-783">If a building file is already uploaded but you need to add missing subnets, do the following in the CQD Tenant Data Upload portal:</span></span>

1.  <span data-ttu-id="73324-784">如果您還沒有最新的複本，請下載原始檔案。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-784">Download the original file, if you don’t already have an up-to-date copy.</span></span>
2.  <span data-ttu-id="73324-785">在 CQD 中移除目前的檔案。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-785">Remove the current file in CQD.</span></span>
3.  <span data-ttu-id="73324-786">將新的子網附加至原始檔案。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-786">Append the new subnets to the original file.</span></span>
4.  <span data-ttu-id="73324-787">上傳組建檔案。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-787">Upload the building file.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-788">請務必先將開始日期設為至少八個月，以便 CQD 會處理歷史資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-788">Be sure to set the start date to at least eight months prior so that CQD will process historical data.</span></span>

### <a name="missing-subnets"></a><span data-ttu-id="73324-789">遺失子網</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-789">Missing subnets</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-790">在您上傳受管理的網路的建築物資訊之後，每個受管理的網路都應該有一個建築物關聯。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-790">After you upload building information for managed networks, every managed network should have a building association.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-791">不過，這不一定是案例;通常會錯過幾個子網。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-791">However, this won’t always be the case; typically, a few subnets are missed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-792">本節涵蓋如何驗證遺失的網路。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-792">This section covers how to validate those missing networks.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-793">流覽至 CQD Online 中的 [**詳細報告**] 頁面，然後流覽至 CQD 範本中包含的**遺失子網報告**。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-793">Browse to the **Detailed Reports** page in CQD Online and navigate to the **Missing Subnet Report** included in the CQD templates.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-794">這會顯示有10個以上的音訊資料流程的所有子網，且未在建築物資料檔中定義，且標示為外部。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-794">This presents all the subnets with 10 or more audio streams that aren’t defined in the building data file and are being marked as outside.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-795">確定此清單中沒有受管理的網路。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-795">Ensure that there are no managed networks in this list.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-796">如果子網遺失，請更新原始的組建資料檔，然後將它重新上傳至 CQD。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-796">If subnets are missing, update the original building data file and re-upload it to CQD.</span></span>

> [!IMPORTANT]
> <span data-ttu-id="73324-797">您必須將您的租使用者識別碼，作為**第二個租使用者識別碼**的查詢篩選器新增至此報告，以篩選報表，以便只查看貴組織的租使用者資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-797">You’ll need to add your tenant ID as a query filter for **Second Tenant ID** to this report to filter the report to view only your organization’s tenant data.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-798">否則，報表就會顯示聯盟子網。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-798">Otherwise, the report will show federated subnets.</span></span>

> [!NOTE] 
> <span data-ttu-id="73324-799">請務必將 [月年度] 報表篩選調整為 [本月]。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-799">Be sure to adjust the Month Year report filter to the current month.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-800">選取 [**編輯**]，然後調整 [**月**] 報表篩選，以儲存新的預設月份。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-800">Select **Edit**, and adjust the **Month Year** report filter to save the new default month.</span></span>

![螢幕擷取畫面顯示遺失的子網報表](media/qerguide-image-missingbuildingreport.png)

<span data-ttu-id="73324-802">_圖 17-缺少建立報告_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-802">_Figure 17 - Missing Building Report_</span></span>

### <a name="building-mapping-tools"></a><span data-ttu-id="73324-803">建立地圖工具</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-803">Building mapping tools</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-804">讓我們來看，在您的組織中有對應的子網，可能相當困難。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-804">Let’s face it, mapping out subnets in your organization can be difficult.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-805">大型全域網路非常複雜，不同的小組管理各自的區域，而且網路拓朴可能沒有單一來源來源。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-805">Large global networks are very complex, with different teams managing their respective regions, and there might be no single source of truth for the network topology.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-806">有兩個工具可用來協助開始建立對應練習，如下列各節所述。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-806">There are two tools available to assist with starting the building mapping exercise, described in the following sections.</span></span>

#### <a name="cqd-tools"></a><span data-ttu-id="73324-807">CQD 工具</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-807">CQD tools</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-808">這些工具都是以 PowerShell 為基礎，而且可以利用 Active Directory （AD）網站和服務與 Microsoft DHCP 服務，協助預先填入您的組建檔案。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-808">These tools are based on PowerShell and can leverage Active Directory (AD) Sites and Services and Microsoft DHCP services to help pre-populate your building file.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="73324-809">這些工具將協助您執行下列任務：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-809">These tools will help with the following tasks:</span></span>

1.  <span data-ttu-id="73324-810">查詢廣告網站和服務，並根據所含的資訊建立組建檔案。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-810">Query AD Sites and Services, and create a building file based on the information contained within.</span></span>
2.  <span data-ttu-id="73324-811">查詢 Microsoft DHCP 伺服器或伺服器以抽取子網資訊並自動建立組建檔案。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-811">Query a Microsoft DHCP server or servers to pull subnet information and automatically create a building file.</span></span>
3.  <span data-ttu-id="73324-812">驗證現有的建築物檔案、檢查重複專案和重疊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-812">Validate an existing building file, checking for duplicates and overlaps.</span></span>
4.  <span data-ttu-id="73324-813">在 CQD 中尋找未對應的子網。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-813">Find unmapped subnets in CQD.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-814">如需此工具的詳細資訊，請參閱[此博客文章](https://aka.ms/cqdtools)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-814">For more information about this tool, see [this blog post](https://aka.ms/cqdtools).</span></span>

#### <a name="network-planner"></a><span data-ttu-id="73324-815">網路 Planner</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-815">Network Planner</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-816">網路 Planner 只需幾個簡單的步驟，就能判斷及組織您雲端語音部署的網路需求。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-816">The Network Planner determines and organizes your network requirements for your Cloud Voice deployment in just a few simple steps.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-817">透過提供貴組織的網路詳細資料和雲端語音使用，您可以大致計算雲端語音部署的網路需求、管理及匯出這些詳細資料以進行報告，以及查看區域以進行進一步調查以及後續步驟。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-817">By providing your organization's networking details and Cloud Voice usage, you can get an approximate calculation of the network requirements for your Cloud Voice deployment, manage and export these details for reporting, and view areas for further investigation and next steps.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-818">雖然網路 Planner 不會完全自動進行組建對應程式，但在網路資訊輸入網路資訊之後，就可以將它匯出至組建檔案，準備好進行上傳。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-818">Although the Network Planner doesn’t automate the building mapping process entirely, after network information is entered into the Network Planner it can then be exported to a building file ready for upload.</span></span>

## <a name="reliability-investigations"></a><span data-ttu-id="73324-819">可靠性調查</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-819">Reliability investigations</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-820">改善品質的第一個步驟是評估整個組織的可靠性狀態。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-820">The first step to improving quality is to assess the state of reliability across the organization.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-821">因為可靠性對於積極的使用者體驗至關重要，所以我們從測量可靠性的兩個元件開始：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-821">Because reliability is vital to a positive user experience, we start with the two components that measure reliability:</span></span>

1.  <span data-ttu-id="73324-822">**安裝失敗：** 無法建立通話。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-822">**Setup failures:** The call couldn’t be established.</span></span>

2.  <span data-ttu-id="73324-823">**Drop 失敗：** 通話已建立且意外終止。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-823">**Drop failures:** The call was established and unexpectedly terminated.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-824">在本節中，我們將說明同時調查兩個區域的方法。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-824">Throughout this section, we’ll cover methods to investigate both areas.</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="73324-825">本指南並未涵蓋範本中包含的所有報表。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-825">Not all reports included in the templates are covered in this guide.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="73324-826">不過，以下所述的調查方法仍適用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-826">However, the methods of investigation explained below still apply.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-827">如需詳細資訊，請參閱個別報表的描述。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-827">Please refer to the individual report description for more information.</span></span>


### <a name="setup-failures"></a><span data-ttu-id="73324-828">設定失敗</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-828">Setup failures</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-829">首先，請優先處理此區域中的修正設定失敗問題，因為這些失敗會對使用者體驗產生嚴重的負面影響。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-829">Prioritize remediating setup failures in this area first, because these failures have a significant negative impact on the user experience.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-830">您可以評估組織的整體設定失敗百分比，然後根據組建或網路最高的百分比來排定調查區域的優先順序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-830">Begin your investigation by assessing the percentage of overall setup failures for the organization, and then prioritize areas of investigation based on the highest percentage by building or network.</span></span> 

#### <a name="setup-failure-trend-analysis"></a><span data-ttu-id="73324-831">設定失敗趨勢分析</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-831">Setup failure trend analysis</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-832">此報告顯示串流的總總量、資料流程設定失敗，以及資料流程設定失敗率。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-832">This report displays the total amount of streams, stream setup failures, and the stream setup failure rate.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-833">指向任何一個資料行，以顯示其個別的值，如下圖所示。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-833">Point to any one of the columns to display its individual values, as shown in the following figure.</span></span> 

![顯示串流設定失敗百分比的圖表](media/qerguide-image-streamsetupfailures.png)

<span data-ttu-id="73324-835">_圖 19-音訊可靠性-資料流程設定失敗_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-835">_Figure 19 - Audio Reliability - Stream Setup Failures_</span></span>

##### <a name="analysis"></a><span data-ttu-id="73324-836">分析</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-836">Analysis</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-837">您可以使用此報告來回答下列問題，並決定您的下一個動作課程：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-837">By using this report, you can answer the following questions and determine your next course of action:</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="73324-838">目前月份的電話設定失敗總百分比是什麼？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-838">What is the total call setup failure percentage for the current month?</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="73324-839">[通話設定失敗] 的總百分比是低於或高於定義的目標度量嗎？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-839">Is the total call setup failure percentage below or above the defined target metric?</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="73324-840">失敗趨勢是否較差或比上個月更佳？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-840">Is the failure trend worse or better than the previous month?</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="73324-841">失敗趨勢是增加、穩定或遞減嗎？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-841">Is the failure trend increasing, steady, or decreasing?</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-842">不論先前的回答如何，請使用隨附子報表來進一步調查，以尋找任何可能需要修正的個別建築物或子網。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-842">Irrespective of the previous answers, take the time to investigate further by using the companion sub-reports to look for any individual buildings or subnets that might need remediation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-843">雖然整體失敗率可能低於目標度量，但一或多個建築物或網路的失敗率可能高於目標指標，且需要調查。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-843">Although the overall failure rate might be below the target metric, the failure rates for one or more buildings or networks might be above the target metric and need investigation.</span></span>

#### <a name="setup-failure-investigations"></a><span data-ttu-id="73324-844">設定失敗調查</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-844">Setup failure investigations</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="73324-845">這個摘要報告是用來探索及隔離任何可能需要修正的建築物或網路。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-845">This summary report is used to discover and isolate any buildings or networks that might need remediation.</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="73324-846">請務必將 [月年度] 報表篩選調整為 [本月]。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-846">Be sure to adjust the Month Year report filter to the current month.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-847">選取 [**編輯**]，然後調整 [**月**] 報表篩選，以儲存新的預設月份。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-847">Select **Edit**, and adjust the **Month Year** report filter to save the new default month.</span></span>
