##### <a name="remediation"></a><span data-ttu-id="73324-850">修正</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-850">Remediation</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="73324-851">將您的第一次修正工作重點放在具有最大大量故障的建築物或子網上。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-851">Focus your first remediation efforts on buildings or subnets that have the largest volume of failures.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-852">這將會最大化對使用者體驗的影響，並有助於快速減少組織電話設定失敗的速度。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-852">This will maximize impact on the user experience and help to quickly reduce the rate of organizational call setup failures.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-853">下表列出由 CQD 報告的設定失敗的兩個原因。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-853">The following table lists the two reasons for setup failures as reported by CQD.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-854">_表 7-通話設定失敗的原因_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-854">_Table 7 – Reasons for Call Setup Failures_</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="73324-855">通話設定失敗的原因</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-855">Call Setup Failures reason</span></span>       | <span data-ttu-id="73324-856">常見的原因</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-856">Typical cause</span></span>                    |
|----------------------------------|----------------------------------|
| <span data-ttu-id="73324-857">遺失固件深層資料包檢查例外規則</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-857">Missing FW Deep Packet Inspection Exemption Rule</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="73324-858">表示由於深入的資料包檢查規則而使媒體路徑無法建立，所以沿著路徑的網路裝置無法進行建立。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-858">Indicates that network equipment along the path prevented the media path from being established due to deep packet inspection rules.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-859">這可能是因為防火牆規則沒有正確設定。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-859">This is likely due to firewall rules not being correctly configured.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-860">在這種情況下，TCP 握手成功，但 SSL 握手沒有。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-860">In this scenario, the TCP handshake succeeded but the SSL handshake didn’t.</span></span>      |
| <span data-ttu-id="73324-861">遺失的 FW IP 封鎖例外規則</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-861">Missing FW IP Block Exception Rule</span></span>      | <span data-ttu-id="73324-862">表示路徑中的網路裝置無法建立媒體路徑給 Office 365 網路。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-862">Indicates that network equipment along the path prevented the media path from being established to the Office 365 network.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-863">這可能是因為無法正確設定 proxy 或防火牆規則，以允許存取用於團隊和商務用 Skype 流量的 IP 位址和埠。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-863">This might be due to proxy or firewall rules not being correctly configured to allow access to IP addresses and ports used for Teams and Skype for Business traffic.</span></span> |

<span data-ttu-id="73324-864">在您開始修正時，您可以將精力集中在特定的建築物或子網上。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-864">Now as you begin your remediation, you can focus your efforts on a particular building or subnet.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-865">如上表所示，這些問題是由防火牆或 proxy 設定所導致。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-865">As the preceding table shows, these issues are due to firewall or proxy configurations.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-866">請參閱下表中的選項，以取得修正動作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-866">Review the options in the following table for remediation actions.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-867">_表格 8-通話設定失敗修正的後續步驟_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-867">_Table 8 - Next Steps for Call Setup Failure Remediation_</span></span>


|      <span data-ttu-id="73324-868">修正</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-868">Remediation</span></span>      |                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   <span data-ttu-id="73324-869">級</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-869">Guidance</span></span>                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   |
|-----------------------|----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| <span data-ttu-id="73324-870">設定防火牆</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-870">Configure firewall(s)</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="73324-871">與您的網路小組合作，並對照[Office 365 IP 位址清單](https://aka.ms/o365ips)驗證您的防火牆設定。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-871">Work with your network team and verify your firewall(s) configuration against [the Office 365 IP address list](https://aka.ms/o365ips).</span></span><br><br><span data-ttu-id="73324-872">確認[媒體子網](https://support.office.com/article/Office-365-URLs-and-IP-address-ranges-8548a211-3fe7-47cb-abb1-355ea5aa88a2#bkmk_teams)和埠都包含在防火牆規則中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-872">Verify that the [media subnets](https://support.office.com/article/Office-365-URLs-and-IP-address-ranges-8548a211-3fe7-47cb-abb1-355ea5aa88a2#bkmk_teams) and ports are included in the firewall rules.</span></span> <br><br><span data-ttu-id="73324-873">確認在防火牆中開啟了必要的埠（如下所示）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-873">Verify that the necessary ports (listed below) are opened in the firewall.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-874">UDP 應該有優先權，因為 TCP 被視為音訊、影片和影片畫面共用的容錯回復通訊協定，而其使用會影響通話品質。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-874">UDP should be given priority because TCP is considered a failback protocol for audio, video, and video-based screen sharing, and its use will affect the quality of the call.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-875">舊版 RDP 應用程式共用只使用 TCP。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-875">Legacy RDP application sharing uses TCP only.</span></span><br><ul><li><span data-ttu-id="73324-876">**TCP：** 埠443</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-876">**TCP:** port 443</span></span></li><li><span data-ttu-id="73324-877">**UDP：** 埠3478–3481</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-877">**UDP:** ports 3478–3481</span></span></li><ul> |
|        <span data-ttu-id="73324-878">是否</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-878">Verify</span></span>         |                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                 <span data-ttu-id="73324-879">使用 [ [Microsoft Network 評](https://www.microsoft.com/download/details.aspx?id=53885)量] 工具，透過連線檢查函數驗證受影響的建築物或子網上的連線性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-879">Use the [Microsoft Network Assessment Tool](https://www.microsoft.com/download/details.aspx?id=53885) to verify connectivity from the affected building or subnet by using the connectivity check function.</span></span>                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  |

### <a name="drop-failures"></a><span data-ttu-id="73324-880">Drop 失敗</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-880">Drop failures</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-881">與 setup 失敗代碼不同的是，CDQ 沒有 drop 失敗程式碼來指出為什麼會發生 drop 失敗，這會讓您難以隔離特定的根本原因。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-881">Unlike setup failure codes, CDQ has no drop failure code to indicate why drop failures occur, which makes it difficult to isolate a specific root cause.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-882">若要更完善的會審放下失敗，請使用推理的方法。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-882">To better triage drop failures, use an inferred approach.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-883">透過修正媒體的任何感興趣區域、修補用戶端和驅動程式，以及推動小組和商務用 Skype 的認證裝置使用量，您可能會想要拒絕丟單失敗。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-883">By remediating any areas of interest for media, patching clients and drivers, and driving usage of certified devices for Teams and Skype for Business, you can expect drop failures to decline.</span></span>

#### <a name="drop-failure-trend-analysis"></a><span data-ttu-id="73324-884">丟單失敗趨勢分析</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-884">Drop failure trend analysis</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-885">此報告顯示音訊流量總量、總丟單失敗次數及擊落失敗率。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-885">This report displays the total amount of audio streams, total drop failures, and the drop failure rate.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-886">指向任何一欄以顯示其值，如下圖所示。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-886">Point to any one of the columns to display its values, as shown in the following figure.</span></span> 

![顯示已丟棄之串流百分比的圖表](media/qerguide-image-droppedstreamrate.png)

##### <a name="analysis"></a><span data-ttu-id="73324-889">分析</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-889">Analysis</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-890">透過使用這種類型的報表，您可以回答下列問題：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-890">By using this type of report, you can answer the following questions:</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="73324-891">目前的擊落失敗率為何？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-891">What is the current drop failure rate?</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="73324-892">Drop 失敗率是否低於定義的目標度量？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-892">Is the drop failure rate below the defined target metric?</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="73324-893">失敗趨勢是否較差或比上個月更佳？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-893">Is the failure trend worse or better than the previous month?</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="73324-894">失敗趨勢是增加、穩定或遞減嗎？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-894">Is the failure trend increasing, steady, or decreasing?</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-895">無論上述問題的答案如何，請花時間調查子報表，以尋找任何可能需要修正的建築物或網路。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-895">Irrespective of the answers to the questions above, take the time to investigate using the sub-reports to look for any buildings or networks that might need remediation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-896">雖然整體 drop 失敗率可能低於目標度量，但一或多個建築物或網路的擊落失敗率可能高於目標指標，且需要調查。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-896">Although the overall drop failure rate might be below the target metric, the drop failure rate for one or more buildings or networks might be above the target metric and need investigation.</span></span>

#### <a name="drop-failure-investigations"></a><span data-ttu-id="73324-897">擊落失敗調查</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-897">Drop failure investigations</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-898">在此報告的失敗指示此通話被意外丟棄，並產生消極的使用者體驗。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-898">Failures reported here indicate that the call was dropped unexpectedly and resulted in a negative user experience.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-899">與趨勢報告不同，這些報告提供其他深入瞭解需要進一步調查之子網的深入見解。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-899">Unlike the trending reports, these reports provide additional insights into specific subnets that need further investigation.</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="73324-900">請務必將 [月份年份] 篩選調整為 [當月]。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-900">Be sure to adjust the Month Year filter to the current month.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-901">選取 [**編輯**]，然後調整**月份年份**以儲存新的預設月份。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-901">Select **Edit**, and adjust **Month Year** to save the new default month.</span></span>

##### <a name="remediation"></a><span data-ttu-id="73324-904">修正</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-904">Remediation</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-905">使用隨附的表格報告，您可以隔離網路中超過您所定義之目標度量的問題區域。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-905">Using the included table reports, you can isolate problem areas in the network where the drop rate is above the target metric you’ve defined.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-906">將您的第一次修正工作重點放在具有最高總串流數的建築物或子網上，以產生最大的影響。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-906">Focus your first remediation efforts on buildings or subnets that have the highest total stream count, to make the biggest impact.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-907">呼叫下降的常見原因：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-907">Common causes of call drops:</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="73324-908">預配的網路或網際網路出口</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-908">Under-provisioned network or internet egress</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="73324-909">受限制的網路上沒有設定 QoS</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-909">No QoS configured on constrained networks</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="73324-910">舊版用戶端版本</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-910">Older client versions</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="73324-911">使用者行為</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-911">User behavior</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-912">在您發現問題區域之後，您可以使用[呼叫分析](https://techcommunity.microsoft.com/t5/Skype-for-Business-Blog/Introducing-Call-Analytics/ba-p/57309)程式進一步查看該組建中的特定問題的使用者。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-912">After you discover your problem areas, you can use [Call Analytics](https://techcommunity.microsoft.com/t5/Skype-for-Business-Blog/Introducing-Call-Analytics/ba-p/57309) to further review users in that building for specific issues.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-913">[通話分析] 包含其他 PII 資料，對於進一步隔離失敗的可能原因，可能會很有用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-913">Call Analytics contains additional PII data and can be useful for further isolating potential reasons for the drop failures.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-914">無論您下一個步驟為何，我們都是一種很好的做法，通知技術台已發現特定建築物或子網的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-914">Regardless of your next step, it’s a good practice to notify the helpdesk that an issue has been discovered with specific buildings or subnets.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-915">如此一來，他們就能快速回應來電，並更有效率地會審使用者。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-915">This way, they can quickly respond to incoming calls and triage users more efficiently.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-916">然後，您可以將已標記的使用者報告回到工程小組，進一步進行調查。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-916">Flagged users can then be reported back to the engineering team for further investigation.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-917">下表列出一些常見的管理與修正失敗的方法。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-917">The following table lists some common methods to manage and remediate drop failures.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-918">_資料表 9-通話刪除修正程式的後續步驟_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-918">_Table 9 - Next steps for call drop remediation_</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="73324-919">修正</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-919">Remediation</span></span>                              | <span data-ttu-id="73324-920">級</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-920">Guidance</span></span>                      |
|------------------------------------------|-------------------------------|
| <span data-ttu-id="73324-921">**Network/網際網路**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-921">**Network/internet**</span></span>                         | <span data-ttu-id="73324-922">**擁塞**：與您的網路小組合作，以監視特定建築物/子網上的頻寬，以確認是否有使用過度的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-922">**Congestion**: Work with your network team to monitor bandwidth at specific buildings/subnets to confirm that there are issues with overutilization.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-923">如果您確認有網路擁塞，請考慮增加建立或應用程式 QoS 的頻寬。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-923">If you do confirm that there is network congestion, consider increasing bandwidth to that building or applying QoS.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-924">使用隨附[品質較差的資料流程摘要報告](#quality-investigations)來查看問題子網，以取得抖動、延遲和資料包遺失的問題，因為這些通常會位於刪除的資料流程前面。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-924">Use the included [Quality Poor Stream summary reports](#quality-investigations) to review the problem subnets for issues with jitter, latency, and packet loss, because these will often precede a dropped stream.</span></span><br><br><span data-ttu-id="73324-925">**QoS**：如果增加頻寬是不切實際或成本不高，請考慮實施 QoS。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-925">**QoS**: If increasing bandwidth is impractical or cost-prohibitive, consider implementing QoS.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-926">這個工具非常適合用來管理擁塞的通訊，並能保證受管理的網路上的媒體資料包在非媒體流量上方的優先順序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-926">This tool is very effective at managing congested traffic and can guarantee that media packets on the managed network are prioritized above non-media traffic.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-927">或者，如果沒有明確的證據證明存在頻寬問題，請考慮下列解決方案：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-927">Alternatively, if there’s no clear evidence that bandwidth is the culprit, consider these solutions:</span></span><ul><li>[<span data-ttu-id="73324-928">Microsoft 團隊 QoS 指導方針</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-928">Microsoft Teams QoS guidance</span></span>](qos-in-teams.md)</li></ul><br><span data-ttu-id="73324-929">**執行網路準備情況評估**：網路評量提供預期頻寬使用量的詳細資料，以及如何處理頻寬和網路變更，以及團隊與商務用 Skype 的建議網路使用做法。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-929">**Perform a network readiness assessment**: A network assessment provides details about expected bandwidth usage, how to cope with bandwidth and network changes, and recommended networking practices for Teams and Skype for Business.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-930">使用上一個資料表做為您的來源，您有一份代表最佳候選評估的建築物或子網清單。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-930">Using the preceding table as your source, you have a list of buildings or subnets that are excellent candidates for an assessment.</span></span><ul><li>[<span data-ttu-id="73324-931">Microsoft 團隊網路準備情況評估</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-931">Microsoft Teams Network Readiness Assessment</span></span>](3-envision-evaluate-my-environment.md#test-the-network)</li></ul><br><span data-ttu-id="73324-932">**Microsoft 網路評估工具：** 您可以使用這個工具進行網路效能的簡單測試，以判斷網路對於團隊或商務用 Skype Online 通話的效果。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-932">**Microsoft Network Assessment Tool:** Use this tool for a simple test of network performance to determine how well the network would perform for a Teams or Skype for Business Online call.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-933">此工具可協助您評估子網的效能，並對照 Microsoft 效能[需求](https://aka.ms/performancerequirements)驗證網路是否已就緒。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-933">The tool helps you assess the performance of a subnet and validate the readiness of the network against Microsoft performance [requirements](https://aka.ms/performancerequirements).</span></span><ul><li>[<span data-ttu-id="73324-934">下載網路評量工具</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-934">Download the Network Assessment Tool</span></span>](https://www.microsoft.com/download/details.aspx?id=53885)</li></ul> |
| <span data-ttu-id="73324-935">**用戶端（僅適用于商務用 Skype Online）**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-935">**Clients (Skype for Business Online only)**</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="73324-936">某些舊版的用戶端有已知的媒體可靠性問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-936">Some older clients have known, documented issues with media reliability.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-937">查看來自多個受影響使用者的呼叫分析報告，或在 CQD 中建立自訂用戶端版本表格報告</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-937">Review the Call Analytics reports from multiple affected users, or create a custom Client Version table report in CQD filtered to specific buildings or subnets with Total Call Dropped Failure % measure.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-938">這項資訊將協助您瞭解該特定建築物與特定用戶端版本中的呼叫中斷之間是否存在關聯性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-938">This information will help you understand whether a relationship exists between call drops in that specific building and a specific version of the client.</span></span>     |
| <span data-ttu-id="73324-939">**裝置**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-939">**Devices**</span></span>                                  | <span data-ttu-id="73324-940">我們建議有任何呼叫中斷的使用者，或一般的呼叫，而且使用整合裝置，都應該提供[經過認證的耳機或免持聽筒](https://partnersolutions.skypeforbusiness.com/solutionscatalog/personal-peripherals-pcs)，將這項功能排除在品質與可靠性上的潛在來源上。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-940">We recommend that any users who are experiencing call drops—or poor calls in general—and are using integrated devices should be provisioned a [certified headset or speakerphone](https://partnersolutions.skypeforbusiness.com/solutionscatalog/personal-peripherals-pcs)  to eliminate this as a potential source of poor quality and reliability.</span></span> |
| <span data-ttu-id="73324-941">**使用者行為**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-941">**User behavior**</span></span>                            | <span data-ttu-id="73324-942">如果您認為網路、裝置或用戶端都不是問題，請考慮開發使用者採用戰略，教育使用者如何最好地加入和結束會議。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-942">If you determine that neither network, devices, or clients are the issue, consider developing a user adoption strategy to educate users how to best join and exit meetings.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-943">更聰明的團隊和商務用 Skype 使用者將能為會議中的所有參與者提供較佳的使用者體驗。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-943">A smarter Teams and Skype for Business user will produce a better user experience for all participants in the meeting.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-944">如果使用者將其膝上型電腦設為睡眠（關閉蓋子）而不離開會議，則會將其分類為意外的呼叫下沉。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-944">A user who puts their laptop to sleep (by closing the lid) without exiting the meeting will be classified as an unexpected call drop.</span></span>   |

## <a name="quality-investigations"></a><span data-ttu-id="73324-945">品質調查</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-945">Quality investigations</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-946">在組織中，評估音訊品質狀態的下一個步驟是調查不良的串流速率（PSR.EXE）、TCP 和 proxy 使用方式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-946">The next step to assess the state of audio quality across the organization is to investigate Poor Stream Rate (PSR), TCP, and proxy usage.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-947">請務必記住，CQD 資料並不會提供特定的根本原因，而是提供可能的問題區域，以與適當的小組開始合作，以取得修正活動。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-947">It’s important to remember that CQD data doesn’t provide you a specific root cause, but instead provides you with likely problem areas to begin a collaborative conversation with the appropriate teams for remediation activities.</span></span> 

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="73324-948">本指南並未涵蓋範本中包含的所有報表。不過，以下所述的調查方法仍適用于這些報表。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-948">Not all reports included in the templates are covered in this guide; however, the methods of investigation explained below will still apply for those reports.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-949">如需詳細資訊，請參閱個別報表的描述。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-949">Refer to the individual report description for more information.</span></span> 

### <a name="quality"></a><span data-ttu-id="73324-950">品質</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-950">Quality</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-951">PSR.EXE 百分比可用來指出組織是否為指定焦點區域的會議定義指標目標。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-951">The PSR percentages are used to indicate whether the organization is meeting defined metric targets for a given focus area.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-952">請務必注意，即使高層百分比位於定義的目標中，個別的子網或建築物可能不符合已定義的目標，因此需要進一步調查。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-952">It’s important to note that even if the high-level percentages are within the defined target, individual subnets or buildings might not meet the defined targets and, therefore, need further investigation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-953">例如，如果整個音訊 PSR.EXE 百分比是4月的2% （符合樣本目標），個別的建築物和子網可能仍會有較差的體驗，這取決於這2% 的整體分佈情況。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-953">For example, if the overall audio PSR percentage is 2 percent in April, which meets the sample target, individual buildings and subnets might still be having poor experiences, depending on the overall distribution of that 2 percent.</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="73324-954">若要評估不良資料流程的百分比，請使用品質報告。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-954">To assess the percentage of poor streams, use the quality reports.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-955">提供各種品質報告來審查整個、會議、二方、PSTN 通話、VPN 和會議室的規格。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-955">Various quality reports are provided to review metrics for overall, conferencing, two-party, PSTN calling, VPN, and meeting rooms.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-956">提供每月、每週及每日報告以協助此處理程式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-956">Monthly, weekly, and daily reports are provided to assist in this process.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-957">每週和每日報告都受限於受管理的網路範本，以提高其效能並減少雜色。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-957">Weekly and daily reports are limited to the Managed Networks template to increase their effectiveness and reduce noise.</span></span> 

#### <a name="quality-trend-analysis"></a><span data-ttu-id="73324-958">品質趨勢分析</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-958">Quality trend analysis</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-959">[趨勢報告] 會隨著時間顯示品質資訊，並用於協助識別並瞭解每個興趣領域內的品質趨勢。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-959">Trending reports display quality information over time and are used to help identify and understand quality trends within each area of interest.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-960">如上所述，範本中有一些報告樹，可用於調查品質;會議、二方、PSTN 通話、VPN 和會議室。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-960">As noted above, there are report trees included in the templates for investigating quality; conferencing, two-party, PSTN calling, VPN, and meeting rooms.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-961">針對分析品質而言，調查程式是一樣的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-961">For the purposes of analyzing quality, the investigative process is the same.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-962">不過，我們建議您先開始使用會議，因為會議品質的任何改善也會對所有其他區域產生積極的影響。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-962">However, we recommend that you start with conferencing first, because any improvements in conference quality will also positively affect all other areas.</span></span> 

> [!Note]
> <span data-ttu-id="73324-963">調查兩方、PSTN 通話和會議室與調查會議類似。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-963">Investigating two-party, PSTN calling, and meeting rooms are similar to investigating conferencing.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-964">焦點是 isloate 具有最差品質的建築物或子網，並找出品質不佳的原因。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-964">The focus is to isloate buildings or subnets that have the worst quality and identify the reason for the poor quality.</span></span>

> [!Important]
> <span data-ttu-id="73324-965">VPN 式報告是使用第二個 VPN 維度來篩選。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-965">VPN-based reports are filtered by using the Second VPN dimension.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-966">這個維度要求 VPN 網路介面卡正確地註冊為遠端存取配接器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-966">This dimension requires that the VPN network adapter be properly registered as a Remote Access Adapter.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-967">VPN 廠商無法可靠地使用這個標誌，而且您的里程會根據貴組織部署的 VPN 供應商而有所不同。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-967">VPN vendors don’t reliably use this flag, and your mileage will vary depending on the VPN vendor deployed at your organization.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-968">如需使用建築物或網路名稱來修改 VPN 報告，請依照[本指南前面](#vpn)所述的指導方針進行。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-968">Follow the guidance outlined [earlier in this guide](#vpn) for modifying the VPN reports if needed by using the building or network name.</span></span>

##### <a name="investigation"></a><span data-ttu-id="73324-971">研究</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-971">Investigation</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-972">您可以使用這些報表，回答下列問題：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-972">By using these reports, you can answer the following questions:</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="73324-973">目前的月份總 PSR.EXE 是什麼？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-973">What is the total PSR for the current month?</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="73324-974">PSR.EXE 是否在定義的目標度量以下？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-974">Is the PSR below the defined target metric?</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="73324-975">PSR.EXE 比上個月更糟或變得更好嗎？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-975">Is PSR worse or better than the previous month?</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="73324-976">PSR.EXE 趨勢是增加、穩定或遞減嗎？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-976">Is the PSR trend increasing, steady, or decreasing?</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-977">無論上述問題的答案如何，您都可以使用子報表來尋找任何可能需要調查的建築物或子網，以取得調查的時間。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-977">Irrespective of the answers to the questions above, take the time to investigate by using the sub-reports to look for any buildings or subnets that might need investigation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-978">雖然整體 PSR.EXE 可能低於目標度量，但一或多個建築物或網路的 PSR.EXE，通常是指標及需求修正。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-978">Although the overall PSR might be below the target metric, often the PSR for one or more buildings or networks is above the metric and needs remediation.</span></span>

#### <a name="quality-investigations"></a><span data-ttu-id="73324-979">品質調查</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-979">Quality investigations</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-980">[品質摘要] 報告可讓您深入瞭解如何將串流分類為較差，並有助於隔離受管理網路中的問題區域。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-980">The quality summary reports give you deeper insight into what contributed to the streams’ being classified as poor and helps to isolate problem areas in the managed network.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-981">雖然所使用的尺寸可能會稍有不同，但每個報告都會包含總數據流、PSR.EXE 和品質不佳等的量值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-981">Although the dimensions used might differ slightly between report, each report will include measures for total streams, total poor streams, PSR, and poor quality due to.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-982">已針對每一個感興趣的領域建立報告：會議、二方、PSTN 通話、VPN 和會議室。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-982">Reports have been created for each area of interest: conferencing, two-party, PSTN calling, VPN, and meeting rooms.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-983">受管理的網路範本包含其他報告，可利用透過組建檔案上傳的位置資訊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-983">The Managed Network template includes additional reports to take advantage of the location information uploaded via the building file.</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="73324-984">請務必將 [月份年份] 篩選調整為 [當月]。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-984">Be sure to adjust the Month Year filter to the current month.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-985">選取 [**編輯**]，然後調整**月份年份**以儲存新的預設月份。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-985">Select **Edit**, and adjust **Month Year** to save the new default month.</span></span>

> [!Note]
> <span data-ttu-id="73324-986">常見的子網難以進行會審，因為其廣泛使用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-986">Common subnets are difficult to triage due to their widespread use.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-987">顯示用戶端公用 IP （第二個自反局域 IP）的個別報告已新增至 [所有網路] 範本，以協助使用常見網路的修正辦公室。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-987">A separate report that displays the client’s public IP (Second Reflexive Local IP) has been added to the All Networks template to assist with remediating offices that use common networks.</span></span>


![螢幕擷取畫面顯示不佳的音訊資料流程摘要](media/qerguide-image-poorqualitysummary.png)

<span data-ttu-id="73324-989">_圖 24-透過建立和子網會議摘要來降低音訊資料流程摘要_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-989">_Figure 24 – Poor Audio Stream Summary by Building and Subnet - Conferencing_</span></span>

##### <a name="remediation"></a><span data-ttu-id="73324-990">修正</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-990">Remediation</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-991">將修正工作集中在具有最大大量資料流程的建築物或子網上，因為這可讓您獲得最大的影響，並有助於快速改善使用者體驗。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-991">Focus your remediation efforts on buildings or subnets that have the largest volume of streams, because this will maximize impact and help to improve the user experience quickly.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-992">使用抖動、資料包遺失及往返時間（RTT）測量來瞭解品質不佳的問題（可能會有一個以上的問題）：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-992">Use the jitter, packet loss, and round-trip time (RTT) measurements to understand what’s contributing to the poor quality (it’s possible for there to be more than one problem):</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="73324-993">**抖動**：媒體資料包的使用速度可能不同，從而導致喇叭音效機器人。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-993">**Jitter**: Media packets are arriving at different speeds, which causes a speaker to sound robotic.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="73324-994">**資料包遺失**：媒體資料包遭到刪除，這會造成遺失文字或音節的效果。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-994">**Packet loss**: Media packets are being dropped, which creates the effect of missing words or syllables.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="73324-995">**RTT**：媒體資料包需要花很長的時間才能取得目的地，這會建立 walkie talkie 的效果。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-995">**RTT**: Media packets are taking a long time to get to their destination, which creates a walkie-talkie effect.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-996">若要協助您調查品質問題，您可以利用[呼叫分析](https://techcommunity.microsoft.com/t5/Skype-for-Business-Blog/Introducing-Call-Analytics/ba-p/57309)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-996">To assist your investigation into quality issues, you can leverage [Call Analytics](https://techcommunity.microsoft.com/t5/Skype-for-Business-Blog/Introducing-Call-Analytics/ba-p/57309).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-997">使用通話分析，您可以查看特定的會議或使用者的詳細通話報告。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-997">With Call Analytics, you can look at a specific conference or users’ detailed call report.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-998">此報告將包含 PII 資料，在您尋找失敗的原因時很有用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-998">This report will contain PII data and is useful when you’re looking for the cause of a failure.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-999">在您知道哪個組建受到影響之後，請直接追蹤該組建中的使用者。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-999">After you know which building is affected, it should be straightforward to track down users in that building.</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="73324-1000">別忘了讓技術支援人員知道這些網路出現品質問題，所以他們可以快速進行會審並回應來電。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1000">Don’t forget to let the helpdesk know that these networks are experiencing quality issues, so they can quickly triage and respond to incoming calls.</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="73324-1002">修正</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1002">Remediation</span></span>                              | <span data-ttu-id="73324-1003">級</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1003">Guidance</span></span>                         |
|------------------------------------------|----------------------------------|
| <span data-ttu-id="73324-1004">**聯網**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1004">**Networks**</span></span>                                 | <span data-ttu-id="73324-1005">**擁塞**：過度使用或未預配的網路可能會導致媒體質量發生問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1005">**Congestion**: An overused or under-provisioned network can cause issues with media quality.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-1006">與網路小組合作，判斷來自使用者的網路連線至網際網路出口點是否有足夠的頻寬支援媒體。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1006">Work with the network team to determine whether the network connections from the user to the internet egress point has enough bandwidth to support media.</span></span> <br><br><span data-ttu-id="73324-1007">**執行網路準備情況評估**：網路評量提供預期頻寬使用量的詳細資料，以及如何處理頻寬和網路變更，以及團隊與商務用 Skype 的建議網路使用做法。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1007">**Perform a network readiness assessment**: A network assessment provides details about expected bandwidth usage, how to cope with bandwidth and network changes, and recommended networking practices for Teams and Skype for Business.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-1008">使用上一個資料表做為您的來源，您有一份代表最佳候選評估的建築物或子網清單。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1008">Using the preceding table as your source, you have a list of buildings or subnets that are excellent candidates for an assessment.</span></span><ul><li>[<span data-ttu-id="73324-1009">Microsoft 團隊網路準備情況評估</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1009">Microsoft Teams Network Readiness Assessment</span></span>](3-envision-evaluate-my-environment.md#test-the-network)</li></ul><br><span data-ttu-id="73324-1010">**Microsoft 網路評估工具：** 您可以使用這個工具進行網路效能的簡單測試，以判斷網路對於團隊或商務用 Skype Online 通話的效果。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1010">**Microsoft Network Assessment Tool:** Use this tool for a simple test of network performance to determine how well the network would perform for a Teams or Skype for Business Online call.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-1011">此工具可協助您評估子網的效能，並對照 Microsoft 效能[需求](https://aka.ms/performancerequirements)驗證網路是否已就緒。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1011">The tool helps you assess the performance of a subnet and validate the readiness of the network against Microsoft performance [requirements](https://aka.ms/performancerequirements).</span></span><ul><li>[<span data-ttu-id="73324-1012">下載網路評量工具</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1012">Download the Network Assessment Tool</span></span>](https://www.microsoft.com/download/details.aspx?id=53885)</li></ul><br> |
| <span data-ttu-id="73324-1013">**服務品質 (QoS)**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1013">**Quality of Service (QoS)**</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="73324-1014">QoS 是一種行之有效的工具，可協助您在擁擠的網路上劃分資料包優先順序，以確保它們的目的地和時間都保持不變。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1014">QoS is a proven tool to help prioritize packets on a congested network to ensure they arrive at their destination intact and on time.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-1015">考慮在整個組織中實現 QoS，以最大限度地提高頻寬限制的使用者體驗品質。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1015">Consider implementing QoS across your organization to maximize the quality of the user experience where bandwidth is constrained.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-1016">QoS 將協助解決與大量資料包遺失相關的問題，以及減少抖動與往返時間等問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1016">QoS will help solve issues typically associated with high levels of packet loss, and—to a lesser degree—jitter and round-trip times.</span></span><ul><li>[<span data-ttu-id="73324-1017">Microsoft 團隊 QoS 指導方針</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1017">Microsoft Teams QoS guidance</span></span>](qos-in-teams.md)</li></ul> |
| <span data-ttu-id="73324-1018">**Wi-fi**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1018">**Wi-Fi**</span></span>               | <span data-ttu-id="73324-1019">Wi-fi 可能會對通話品質產生很大的影響。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1019">Wi-Fi can have a significant impact on call quality.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-1020">Wi-fi 部署通常不會考慮 VoIP 服務的網路需求，而且通常是品質較差的來源。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1020">Wi-Fi deployments don’t typically take into consideration the network requirements for VoIP services and are often a source of poor quality.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-1021">如需優化 Wi-fi 基礎結構的詳細資訊，請參閱[這篇有關 wi-fi 規劃的文章](/skypeforbusiness/certification/plan-wifi)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1021">For more information about optimizing your Wi-Fi infrastructure, see [this article about Wi-Fi planning](/skypeforbusiness/certification/plan-wifi).</span></span><br><br><span data-ttu-id="73324-1022">**無線驅動程式**：確認無線驅動程式是最新的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1022">**Wireless driver**: Ensure that wireless drivers are up to date.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-1023">這將有助於降低與過時的驅動程式相關的任何較差的使用者經驗。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1023">This will help mitigate any poor user experience related to an outdated driver.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-1024">許多組織在其修補程式週期中不會包含無線驅動程式，而且這些驅動程式在幾年後可能會有修補程式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1024">Many organizations don’t include wireless drivers in their patch cycles, and these drivers can go unpatched for years.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-1025">許多無線問題都是透過確保無線驅動程式是最新的方式來解決。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1025">Many wireless issues are solved by ensuring the wireless drivers are up to date.</span></span><br><br><span data-ttu-id="73324-1026">**WMM**：無線多媒體擴充（WMM）又稱為 wi-fi 多媒體，提供無線網路的基本 QoS 功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1026">**WMM**: Wireless Multimedia Extensions (WMM), also known as Wi-Fi Multimedia, provides basic QoS features to wireless networks.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-1027">現代無線網路必須支援許多裝置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1027">Modern wireless networks must support many devices.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-1028">這些裝置會爭用頻寬，而且可能會造成 VoIP 服務的品質問題，其中的速度與延遲是至關重要的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1028">These devices compete for bandwidth and can lead to quality issues for VoIP services, where speed and latency are vital.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-1029">請諮詢您的無線轉銷商以取得詳細資訊，並考慮在無線網路上實施 WMM，以排定商務用 Skype 與團隊媒體的優先順序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1029">Consult your wireless vendor for specifics and consider implementing WMM on your wireless network to prioritize Skype for Business and Teams media.</span></span><br><br><span data-ttu-id="73324-1030">**存取點密度**：存取點可能太遠，或不在理想的位置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1030">**Access point density**: Access points might be too far apart or not in an ideal location.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-1031">若要將潛在干擾降至最低，請在會議室中放置額外的存取點，並在不受牆壁或其他物件（也就是弱類型的位置）中放入較弱的位置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1031">To minimize potential interference, place extra access points in conference rooms and in locations that aren’t obstructed by walls or other objects where the Wi-Fi signal is weak.</span></span><br><br><span data-ttu-id="73324-1032">**2.4 ghz 與 5 ghz**： 5 ghz 可提供較低的背景干擾與較高的速度，以及在使用 Wi-fi 部署 VoIP 時應優先的優先順序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1032">**2.4 GHz versus 5 GHz**: 5 GHz provides less background interference and higher speeds, and should be prioritized when deploying VoIP over Wi-Fi.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-1033">不過，5 GHz 與 2.4 GHz 不一樣，也不會輕易滲透牆。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1033">However, 5 GHz isn’t as strong as 2.4 GHz and doesn’t penetrate walls as easily.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-1034">請檢查您的組建版面配置，判斷您可以信賴哪個頻率來取得最佳連接。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1034">Review your building layout to determine which frequency you can rely on for the best connection.</span></span> |
|<span data-ttu-id="73324-1035">**網路裝置**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1035">**Network device**</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="73324-1036">較大型的組織可能會有成百上千個裝置分佈在網路上。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1036">Larger organizations might have hundreds of devices spread out across the network.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-1037">與您的網路小組共同作業，以確保使用者的網路裝置和網際網路都能維持在最新狀態。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1037">Work with your network team to ensure that the network devices from the user to the internet are maintained and up to date.</span></span> |
| <span data-ttu-id="73324-1038">**點對點**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1038">**VPN**</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="73324-1039">VPN 裝置並未傳統設計來處理即時媒體工作負載。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1039">VPN appliances aren’t traditionally designed to handle real-time media workloads.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-1040">某些 VPN 設定會禁止使用 UDP （這是媒體的首選通訊協定），而且只依賴 TCP。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1040">Some VPN configurations prohibit the use of UDP (which is the preferred protocol for media) and rely on TCP only.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-1041">考慮實現 VPN 分割隧道解決方案，以協助將 VPN 減少為品質較差的來源。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1041">Consider implementing a VPN split-tunnel solution to help reduce VPN as a source of poor quality.</span></span> |
| <span data-ttu-id="73324-1042">**台**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1042">**Clients**</span></span> <br><span data-ttu-id="73324-1043">（僅適用于商務用 Skype Online）</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1043">(Skype for Business Online only)</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="73324-1044">確保定期更新所有用戶端。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1044">Ensure all clients are being regularly updated.</span></span> |
| <span data-ttu-id="73324-1045">**裝置**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1045">**Devices**</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="73324-1046">使用優化的[裝置](https://partnersolutions.skypeforbusiness.com/solutionscatalog)有助於大大改善使用者體驗。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1046">The use of [optimized devices](https://partnersolutions.skypeforbusiness.com/solutionscatalog) can help to significantly improve the user experience.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-1047">隨著所有專案的需求，優化的裝置會設計成最大化團隊和商務用 Skype 的使用者體驗，並產生優質的品質。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1047">With all things being equal, optimized devices are designed to maximize the user experience with Teams and Skype for Business, and produce superior quality.</span></span> |
| <span data-ttu-id="73324-1048">**驅動程式**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1048">**Drivers**</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="73324-1049">修補網路（乙太網與 Wi-fi）、音訊、影片和 USB 驅動程式都應該是整個修補程式管理原則的一部分。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1049">Patching network (Ethernet and Wi-Fi), audio, video, and USB drivers should be part of your overall patch management strategy.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-1050">更新驅動程式可解決許多品質問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1050">Many quality issues are solved by updating drivers.</span></span> |
| <span data-ttu-id="73324-1051">**Wi-fi 上的會議室**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1051">**Meeting rooms on Wi-Fi**</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="73324-1052">我們強烈建議您使用至少 1 Gbps 乙太網連線，將會議室裝置連線至網路。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1052">We highly recommend that meeting room devices be connected to the network by using at least a 1-Gbps Ethernet connection.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-1053">會議室裝置通常包含多個音訊與影片流量，以及會議內容（例如螢幕共用），並具有比其他團隊或商務用 Skype 端點更高的網路需求。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1053">Meeting room devices typically include multiple audio and video streams, along with meeting content such as screen sharing, and have higher network requirements than other Teams or Skype for Business endpoints.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-1054">依定義，會議室只會在安裝期間提供福利的固定裝置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1054">Meeting rooms are, by definition, stationary devices where Wi-Fi affords a benefit only during installation.</span></span><br><br><span data-ttu-id="73324-1055">會議室需要進行額外的注意與注意，以確保使用這些裝置的體驗達到或超過預期。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1055">Meeting rooms need to be treated with extra care and attention to ensure that the experience using these devices is meeting or exceeding expectations.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-1056">會議室的品質問題通常會快速上報，因為它們通常是由資深的人員使用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1056">Quality issues with meeting rooms are usually going to be escalated quickly, because they’re often used by senior-level staff.</span></span><br><br><span data-ttu-id="73324-1057">所有專案都是同等的（除了便利性之外），Wi-fi 效能通常小於有線連線。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1057">With all things being equal (apart from convenience), Wi-Fi performance is often less than a wired connection.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-1058">隨著「攜帶您自己的裝置」原則以及膝上型電腦的急劇增加，您通常會使用 Wi-fi 存取點。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1058">With the rise of “bring your own device” policies and the proliferation of laptops, Wi-Fi access points are often over-utilized.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-1059">即時媒體可能不會在 Wi-fi 網路上劃分優先順序，這可能會在高峰使用時間導致品質問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1059">Real-time media might not be prioritized on Wi-Fi networks, which can lead to quality issues during peak use times.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-1060">這種繁重的使用方式可能會與會議中有十二人的會議相符，每個人都有自己的膝上型電腦和智慧型手機，而且都與會議室裝置連線到相同的 Wi-fi 存取點。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1060">This heavy usage can coincide with a meeting where there might be a dozen people in attendance, each with their own laptop and smartphone, all connected to the same Wi-Fi access point as the meeting room device.</span></span><br><br><span data-ttu-id="73324-1061">Wi-fi 只能看作是針對行動安裝的暫時解決方案，或在已正確設定 Wi-fi 以支援商務級即時媒體的情況下使用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1061">Wi-Fi should only be considered as a temporary solution, for a mobile installation, or when Wi-Fi has been properly provisioned to support business-class, real-time–based media.</span></span> |


### <a name="tcp"></a><span data-ttu-id="73324-1062">TCP-OUT</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1062">TCP</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-1063">TCP 被視為 [回切傳輸]，而不是您想要用於即時媒體的主要傳輸。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1063">TCP is considered a failback transport and not the primary transport you want for real-time media.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-1064">因為 TCP 的全狀態性質，所以它是回切傳輸的原因。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1064">The reason it’s a failback transport is due to the stateful nature of TCP.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-1065">例如，如果通話是在潛在的網路上進行，而媒體資料包則是在延遲後的數秒前（這是不再有用的資料包），這會使頻寬更糟，這可能會導致錯誤的情況。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1065">For example, if a call is made on a latent network and media packets are delayed, then packets from a few seconds ago—which are no longer useful—compete for bandwidth to get to the receiver, which can make a bad situation worse.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-1066">這會讓音訊 healer 縫合及伸展音訊，從而產生可聽見的專案，通常是以抖動的形式出現。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1066">This makes the audio healer stitch and stretch audio, resulting in audible artifacts, often in the form of jitter.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-1067">此區段中的報表不會對良好與不良的資料流程產生任何差異。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1067">The reports in this section don’t make a distinction between good and poor streams.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-1068">考慮到 UDP 是可取的，報告會尋找使用 TCP 進行音訊、影片及影片的螢幕共用（VBSS）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1068">Given that UDP is preferred, the reports look for the use of TCP for audio, video, and video-based screen sharing (VBSS).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-1069">提供的串流速率較差是為了協助比較 UDP 品質與 TCP 品質，讓您能專注于最大限度的效果。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1069">Poor stream rates are provided to help compare UDP quality versus TCP quality so that you can focus your efforts where the impact is the greatest.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-1070">TCP 使用量主要是由不完整的防火牆規則所造成。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1070">TCP usage is primarily caused by incomplete firewall rules.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-1071">如需小組和商務用 Skype Online 防火牆規則的詳細資訊，請參閱[Office 365 url 與 IP 位址範圍](https://aka.ms/o365ips)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1071">For more information about firewall rules for Teams and Skype for Business Online, see [Office 365 URLs and IP address ranges](https://aka.ms/o365ips).</span></span>

> [!Important]
> <span data-ttu-id="73324-1072">強烈建議您先上傳[有效的生成](#building-mapping)檔案，讓您可以在查看 TCP 使用方式時，快速區分外部資料流。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1072">Having a [valid building file](#building-mapping) uploaded is highly recommended so you can quickly distinguish inside from outside streams when looking at TCP usage.</span></span>

> [!Note]
> <span data-ttu-id="73324-1073">[音訊]、[影片] 和 [VBSS]，將所有偏好的 UDP 做為主要傳輸。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1073">Audio, video, and VBSS all prefer UDP as their primary transport.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-1074">舊版 RDP 應用程式共用工作負載只使用 TCP。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1074">The legacy RDP Application Sharing workload only uses TCP.</span></span>

#### <a name="tcp-usage"></a><span data-ttu-id="73324-1075">TCP 使用量</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1075">TCP usage</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-1076">TCP 報告表示過去七個月內的整體 TCP 使用量。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1076">TCP reports indicates the overall TCP usage over the last seven months.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-1077">本節中的所有進一步報告將重點向下縮小特定建築物，以及 TCP 最常使用的子網。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1077">All further reports in this section will focus on narrowing down specific buildings and subnets where TCP is most commonly used.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-1078">每個會議和兩方的資料流程都有不同的報表。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1078">Separate reports are available for both conferencing and two-party streams.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-1079">![圖表顯示使用 tcp](media/qerguide-image-audiostreamswithtcp.png)
_圖25（含 tcp 使用的音訊串流）_ 之音訊資料流程的百分比</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1079">![Chart showing the percentage of audio streams that use TCP](media/qerguide-image-audiostreamswithtcp.png)

##### <a name="investigation"></a><span data-ttu-id="73324-1080">研究</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1080">Investigation</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-1081">您可以使用此報告回答下列問題：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1081">By using this report, you can answer the following questions:</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="73324-1082">目前月份的 TCP 資料流程總容量為何？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1082">What is the total volume of TCP streams for the current month?</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="73324-1083">它是否比前個月更糟或變得更好？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1083">Is it worse or better than the previous month?</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="73324-1084">TCP 使用量趨勢是增加、穩定或遞減嗎？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1084">Is the TCP usage trend increasing, steady, or decreasing?</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="73324-1085">TCP PSR.EXE 與我的整體 PSR.EXE 是否相同？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1085">Is the TCP PSR the same as my overall PSR?</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-1086">如果您發現 TCP 使用量趨勢增加或高於正常的每月使用時間，請使用子報表來尋找任何可能需要修正的建築物或網路，以進行調查。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1086">If you notice that the TCP usage trend is increasing or above normal monthly usage, take the time to investigate by using the sub-reports to look for any buildings or networks that might need remediation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-1087">理想的情況是，您想要在受管理的網路上盡可能少進行 TCP 式音訊會話。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1087">Ideally, you want as few TCP-based audio sessions as possible on the managed network.</span></span>

#### <a name="tcp-vs-udp"></a><span data-ttu-id="73324-1088">TCP 與 UDP</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1088">TCP vs. UDP</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-1089">此報告會識別最新月份的 TCP 和 UDP 使用方式報告（VBSS），以及音訊、影片和影片畫面共用（）的數量。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1089">This report identifies the volume of TCP versus UDP usage reporting on the latest month for audio, video, and video-based screen sharing (VBSS).</span></span>

##### <a name="analysis"></a><span data-ttu-id="73324-1092">分析</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1092">Analysis</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-1093">雖然您想要盡可能地降低 TCP 使用量，但您可能會在其他健康的部署中看到一些 TCP 使用量。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1093">Although you want TCP usage to be as low as possible, you might see a bit of TCP usage in an otherwise healthy deployment.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-1094">TCP 本身不會對不佳的呼叫造成影響，因此會提供串流速度，以協助找出 TCP 使用量是否是品質不佳的參與者。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1094">TCP by itself won’t contribute to a poor call, so stream rates are provided to help identify whether TCP usage is a contributor to poor quality.</span></span> 

#### <a name="tcp-investigations"></a><span data-ttu-id="73324-1095">TCP 調查</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1095">TCP investigations</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-1096">在提供的 CQD 範本中，您可以使用 [Managed 網路] 或 [所有網路] 範本來建立和子網報告，流覽至 TCP 資料流程。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1096">In the provided CQD templates, navigate to the TCP Streams by Building and Subnet reports by using either the Managed Networks or All Networks template.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-1097">出於調查 TCP 使用的目的，程式是一樣的，因此我們將重點放在會議上的討論。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1097">For the purpose of investigating TCP usage, the process is the same, so we’ll focus the discussion here on conferencing.</span></span>

> [!IMPORTANT]
> <span data-ttu-id="73324-1098">建議您先上傳有效的[建築物](#building-mapping)檔案，讓您可以在查看 TCP 使用方式時，快速區分外部的資料流程。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1098">Having a valid [building file](#building-mapping) uploaded is recommended so you can quickly distinguish inside from outside streams when looking at TCP usage.</span></span> 

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="73324-1099">請務必將 [月份年份] 篩選調整為 [當月]。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1099">Be sure to adjust the Month Year filter to the current month.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-1100">選取 [**編輯**]，然後調整**月份年份**以儲存新的預設月份。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1100">Select **Edit**, and adjust **Month Year** to save the new default month.</span></span>                                  |

##### <a name="remediation"></a><span data-ttu-id="73324-1103">修正</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1103">Remediation</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-1104">這個報告會識別對 TCP 使用量而言所造成的特定建築物與子網。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1104">This report identifies specific buildings and subnets that are contributing to the volume of TCP usage.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-1105">此外還包含額外的報告，以識別通話中所使用的 Microsoft 中繼 IP，以協助隔離遺失的防火牆規則。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1105">An additional report is also included to identify the Microsoft Relay IP that was used in the call to help isolate missing firewall rules.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-1106">將您的修正工作重點放在那些具有最高 TCP 資料流程的建築物上，以獲得最佳效果。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1106">Focus your remediation efforts on those buildings that have the highest volume of TCP streams to maximize impact.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-1107">TCP 使用的最常見原因是防火牆或 proxy 中缺少例外規則。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1107">The most common cause of TCP usage is missing exception rules in firewalls or proxies.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-1108">我們將在下一節中討論 proxy，所以現在將焦點放在防火牆上。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1108">We’ll be talking about proxies in the next section, so for now focus your efforts on the firewalls.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-1109">使用所提供的建築物或子網，您可以判斷需要更新哪些防火牆。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1109">By using the building or subnet provided, you can determine which firewall needs to be updated.</span></span>


<span data-ttu-id="73324-1110">_資料表11：透過建立和子網來進行 TCP 資料流程修正指南_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1110">_Table 11 - Remediation guidance for TCP streams by building and subnet_</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="73324-1111">修正</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1111">Remediation</span></span>        | <span data-ttu-id="73324-1112">級</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1112">Guidance</span></span>     |
|--------------------|--------------------------------------|
| <span data-ttu-id="73324-1113">設定防火牆</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1113">Configure firewall</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="73324-1114">確認已從您的防火牆中排除[Office 365 IP 埠和位址](https://aka.ms/o365ips)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1114">Verify that [Office 365 IP ports and addresses](https://aka.ms/o365ips) are excluded from your firewall.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-1115">針對媒體相關的 TCP 問題，請將您的初始工作重點放在下列各項：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1115">For media-related TCP issues, focus your initial efforts on the following:</span></span><ul><li><span data-ttu-id="73324-1116">確認用戶端媒體子網 13.107.64.0/18 和 52.112.0.0/14 都在您的防火牆規則中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1116">Verify that the client media subnets 13.107.64.0/18 and 52.112.0.0/14 are in your firewall rules.</span></span></li><li><span data-ttu-id="73324-1117">UDP 埠3478–3481是必要的媒體埠，必須開啟，否則用戶端會傳回 TCP 埠443的故障。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1117">UDP ports 3478–3481 are the required media ports and must be opened, otherwise the client will fail back to TCP port 443.</span></span></li></ul> |
| <span data-ttu-id="73324-1118">是否</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1118">Verify</span></span>             | <span data-ttu-id="73324-1119">使用[Microsoft Network 評量工具](https://www.microsoft.com/download/details.aspx?id=53885)，查看與受影響的建築物或子網上的特定 OFFICE 365 IP 位址與埠的連線問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1119">Use the [Microsoft Network Assessment Tool](https://www.microsoft.com/download/details.aspx?id=53885) to check for issues with connectivity to specific Office 365 IP addresses and ports from the affected building or subnet.</span></span>    |

### <a name="http-proxy"></a><span data-ttu-id="73324-1120">HTTP proxy</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1120">HTTP proxy</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-1121">出於許多原因，HTTP proxy 不是建立媒體會話的首選路徑。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1121">HTTP proxies aren’t the preferred path for establishing media sessions, for a multitude of reasons.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-1122">許多包含可防止服務連線完成並帶來中斷的深資料包檢查功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1122">Many contain deep packet inspection features that can prevent connections to the service from being completed and introduce disruptions.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-1123">此外，幾乎所有的 proxy 都會強制 TCP，而不是允許使用 UDP，這是針對最佳音訊品質所建議的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1123">Additionally, almost all proxies force TCP as opposed to allowing UDP, which is recommended for optimal audio quality.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-1124">我們總是建議您將用戶端設定為直接連線至團隊和商務用 Skype 服務。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1124">We always recommend that you configure the client to directly connect to Teams and Skype for Business services.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-1125">這對於媒體通信量而言尤為重要。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1125">This is especially important for media-based traffic.</span></span>


> [!IMPORTANT]
> <span data-ttu-id="73324-1126">上傳有效的[組建](#building-mapping)檔案可讓您輕鬆地在分析 proxy 使用方式時，在外部音訊資料流程中正確區分。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1126">Having a valid [building file](#building-mapping) uploaded makes it easy to properly distinguish inside from outside audio streams when analyzing proxy usage.</span></span> 


#### <a name="http-proxy-usage"></a><span data-ttu-id="73324-1127">HTTP proxy 使用量</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1127">HTTP proxy usage</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-1128">範本這個區段中的 HTTP proxy 串流報告，與 TCP 報告非常類似。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1128">The HTTP proxy stream report in this section of the template is much like the TCP reports.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-1129">它不會查看通話是否較差或良好，但通話是否是經由 HTTP 連線。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1129">It doesn’t look at whether calls are poor or good, but whether the call is connected over HTTP.</span></span>

![使用 HTTP 之音訊資料流程報告的螢幕擷取畫面](media/qerguide-image-audiostreamswithhttp.png)
