##### <a name="analysis"></a><span data-ttu-id="73324-1132">分析</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1132">Analysis</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-1133">您想要查看盡可能少的 HTTP 媒體資料流程。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1133">You want to see as little HTTP media streams as possible.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-1134">如果您有資料流程遍歷您的 proxy，請諮詢您的網路小組，以確保適當的排除措施正確無誤，讓用戶端直接路由至小組或商務用 Skype Online 媒體子網。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1134">If you have streams traversing your proxy, consult your networking team to ensure that the proper exclusions are in place so that clients are directly routing to Teams or Skype for Business Online media subnets.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-1135">如果您的組織只有一個網際網路 proxy，請確認正確的[Office 365 url 與 IP 位址範圍排除](https://aka.ms/o365ips)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1135">If you have only one internet proxy in your organization, verify the proper [Office 365 URLs and IP address range exclusions](https://aka.ms/o365ips).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-1136">如果您的組織中設定了多個網際網路 proxy，請使用 HTTP 子報表來隔離受影響的建築物或子網。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1136">If more than one internet proxy is configured in your organization, use the HTTP sub-report to isolate which building or subnet is affected.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-1137">對於無法繞過 proxy 的組織而言，請務必將商務用 Skype 用戶端設定為在 proxy 之後正確登入，如商務用 Skype 中所述，請[使用 proxy 伺服器登入，而不是嘗試直接](https://support.microsoft.com/help/3207112/skype-for-business-should-use-proxy-server-to-sign-in-instead-of-tryin)連線。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1137">For organizations that can’t bypass the proxy, ensure that the Skype for Business client is configured to sign in properly when it’s located behind a proxy, as outlined in the article [Skype for Business should use proxy server to sign in instead of trying direct connection](https://support.microsoft.com/help/3207112/skype-for-business-should-use-proxy-server-to-sign-in-instead-of-tryin).</span></span> 


#### <a name="http-proxy-investigations"></a><span data-ttu-id="73324-1138">HTTP proxy 調查</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1138">HTTP proxy investigations</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-1139">此報告會識別出對 HTTP 使用量有影響的特定建築物與子網。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1139">This report identifies specific buildings and subnets that are contributing to HTTP usage.</span></span>

> [!IMPORTANT]
> <span data-ttu-id="73324-1140">上傳有效的[組建](#building-mapping)檔案可讓您輕鬆地在分析 proxy 使用方式時，在外部音訊資料流程中正確區分。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1140">Having a valid [building file](#building-mapping) uploaded makes it easy to properly distinguish inside from outside audio streams when analyzing proxy usage.</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="73324-1141">請務必將 [月份年份] 篩選調整為 [當月]。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1141">Be sure to adjust the Month Year filter to the current month.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-1142">選取 [**編輯**]，然後調整**月份年份**以儲存新的預設月份。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1142">Select **Edit**, and adjust **Month Year** to save the new default month.</span></span>

![透過建立和子網來 Sreen HTTP Proxy 使用方式報告的快照](media/qerguide-image-httpproxyusage.png)

<span data-ttu-id="73324-1144">_圖 29-透過建立和子網來使用 HTTP Proxy_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1144">_Figure 29 – HTTP Proxy Usage by Building and Subnet_</span></span>

##### <a name="remediation"></a><span data-ttu-id="73324-1145">修正</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1145">Remediation</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-1146">我們[建議](proxy-servers-for-skype-for-business-online.md)您永遠都不要針對商務用 Skype 和小組（尤其是媒體流量）略過這些代理。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1146">We [recommend](proxy-servers-for-skype-for-business-online.md) that you always bypass proxies for Skype for Business and Teams, especially media traffic.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-1147">Proxy 不會讓商務用 Skype 更加安全，因為其流量已經過加密。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1147">Proxies don't make Skype for Business more secure, because its traffic is already encrypted.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-1148">效能相關問題可透過延遲與資料包遺失來引進環境。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1148">Performance-related problems can be introduced to the environment through latency and packet loss.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-1149">這類問題將會在即時資料流至關重要的情況下，使用音訊、影片和螢幕共用來產生負面體驗。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1149">Issues such as these will result in a negative experience with audio, video and screen sharing, where real-time streams are essential.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-1150">HTTP 使用的最常見原因是 proxy 中缺少例外規則。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1150">The most common cause of HTTP usage is missing exception rules in proxies.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-1151">使用所提供的建築物或子網，您可以快速判斷需要為媒體旁路設定哪些 proxy。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1151">By using the building or subnet provided, you can quickly determine which proxy needs to be configured for media bypass.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-1152">確認您的 proxy 中有必要的[Office 365 fqdn](https://aka.ms/o365ips)是列入白名單。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1152">Verify that the required [Office 365 FQDNs](https://aka.ms/o365ips) are whitelisted in your proxy.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-1153">如需有關在商務用 Skype Online 和小組中使用 proxy 的詳細資訊，[請參閱本文](proxy-servers-for-skype-for-business-online.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1153">For more information about using proxies with Skype for Business Online and Teams, see [this article](proxy-servers-for-skype-for-business-online.md).</span></span>

## <a name="endpoint-investigations"></a><span data-ttu-id="73324-1154">端點調查</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1154">Endpoint investigations</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-1155">本節重點針對用戶端版本的報告工作，以及使用已認證的裝置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1155">This section is focused on the tasks for reporting on client versions and the use of certified devices.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-1156">您可以在用戶端版本、用戶端類型、擷取裝置與驅動程式（麥克風）、影片捕獲裝置以及 Wi-fi 供應商和驅動程式版本的大綱用法中使用報告。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1156">Reports are available to outline usage for client versions, client type, capture devices and drivers (microphone), video capture devices, and Wi-Fi vendor and driver versions.</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="73324-1157">本指南並未涵蓋範本中包含的所有報表。不過，以下所述的調查方法仍適用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1157">Not all reports included in the templates are covered in this guide; however, the methods of investigation explained below still apply.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-1158">如需詳細資訊，請參閱個別報表的描述。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1158">Refer to the individual report description for more information.</span></span>

### <a name="client-versions"></a><span data-ttu-id="73324-1159">用戶端版本</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1159">Client versions</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-1160">此空間中的報告主要是識別使用中的商務用 Skype 用戶端版本，以及其在環境中的相對量。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1160">The reports in this space focus on identifying Skype for Business client versions in use and their relative volume in the environment.</span></span>

> [!IMPORTANT]
> <span data-ttu-id="73324-1161">目前，團隊用戶端會透過 Azure 內容傳遞網路自動發佈並更新，並將由服務保持最新狀態。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1161">Currently, Teams clients are distributed and updated automatically through the Azure Content Delivery Network and will be kept up to date by the service.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-1162">用戶端準備與調查活動不適用於小組。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1162">Client readiness and investigative activities aren’t applicable to Teams.</span></span>

> [!Important]
> <span data-ttu-id="73324-1163">除非您排除聯盟參與者資料，否則這些報告將包含來自聯盟端點的用戶端遙測。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1163">Unless you exclude federated participant data, these reports will include client telemetry from federated endpoints.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-1164">若要排除同盟端點，您必須在您組織的[租使用者識別碼](#tenant-id)中，新增第二個租使用者 id 的[查詢篩選器](#query-filters)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1164">To exclude federated endpoints, you must add a [query filter](#query-filters) for Second Tenant ID set to your organization’s [tenant ID](#tenant-id).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-1165">或者，您也可以使用[URL 篩選](#url-filter)來排除同盟參與者遙測。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1165">Alternatively, you can use a [URL filter](#url-filter) to exclude federated participant telemetry.</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="73324-1166">請務必將 [月份年份] 篩選調整為 [當月]。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1166">Be sure to adjust the Month Year filter to the current month.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-1167">選取 [**編輯**]，然後調整**月份年份**以儲存新的預設月份。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1167">Select **Edit**, and adjust **Month Year** to save the new default month.</span></span>

![用戶端與裝置報告的螢幕擷取畫面](media/qerguide-image-clientversionreport.png)

<span data-ttu-id="73324-1169">_圖 30-用戶端版本報告_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1169">_Figure 30 - Client version report_</span></span>

#### <a name="remediation"></a><span data-ttu-id="73324-1170">修正</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1170">Remediation</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-1171">驅動高品質的使用者體驗的重要部分是，確保受管理的用戶端執行的是最新版本的商務用 Skype，除了可確保支援的音訊、影片、網路及 USB 驅動程式都是最新版本。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1171">A critical part of driving high-quality user experiences is ensuring that managed clients are running up-to-date versions of Skype for Business, in addition to ensuring the supporting audio, video, network, and USB drivers are up to date.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-1172">這提供數個優點，其中包括：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1172">This provides several benefits, among them:</span></span> 

-   <span data-ttu-id="73324-1173">更容易管理幾個版本，與許多版本相比。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1173">It’s easier to manage a few versions versus many versions.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="73324-1174">它提供經驗的一致性等級。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1174">It provides a level of consistency of experience.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="73324-1175">它可讓您更輕鬆地排查通話品質和可用性問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1175">It makes it easier to troubleshoot problems with call quality and usability.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="73324-1176">Microsoft 會持續進行整個產品的一般改善及優化。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1176">Microsoft continually makes general improvements and optimizations across the product.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-1177">確保使用者收到這些更新，會降低遇到已解決問題的風險。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1177">Ensuring that users receive these updates reduces their risk of running into a problem that has already been solved.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-1178">將您的部署限制在超過六個月之前的用戶端版本，將可減少所需支援的版本數，改善使用者的整體體驗並改善易管理性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1178">Limiting your deployment to client versions that are less than six months old will improve the overall user experience and improve manageability by reducing the number of versions that need to be supported.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-1179">如果您使用的是 Office 隨選即用，您會自動在六個月內的視窗中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1179">If you’re using only Office Click-to-Run, you’ll automatically be within the six-month window.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-1180">不需要進一步的動作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1180">No further action is required.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-1181">如果您有混合的隨選即用與安裝程式套件（MSI），您可以使用報告來確認 MSI 用戶端定期更新。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1181">If you have a mix of Click-to-Run and installer packages (MSI), you can use the report to verify that the MSI clients are being updated regularly.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-1182">如果您發現用戶端落後，請與負責管理 Office 更新的小組合作，並確定他們要定期核准和部署用戶端修補程式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1182">If you notice clients are falling behind, work with the team responsible for managing Office updates and ensure that they’re approving and deploying client patches regularly.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-1183">您也必須考慮並確保網路、影片、USB 和音訊驅動程式也有修補。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1183">It’s also important to consider and ensure that the network, video, USB, and audio drivers are being patched as well.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-1184">您可以輕鬆地忽略這些驅動程式，而不要將它們包含在您的修補程式管理原則中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1184">It can be easy to overlook these drivers and not include them in your patch management strategy.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-1185">您可以透過下列連結找到商務用 Skype 的版本號碼：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1185">Version numbers for Skype for Business can be found via the links below:</span></span>

-   [<span data-ttu-id="73324-1186">Office 專業增強版更新的發行資訊</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1186">Release information for updates to Office ProPlus</span></span>](https://docs.microsoft.com/officeupdates/release-notes-office365-proplus)
-   [<span data-ttu-id="73324-1187">Office 365 專業增強版的更新歷程記錄</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1187">Update history for Office 365 ProPlus</span></span>](https://docs.microsoft.com/officeupdates/update-history-office365-proplus-by-date)
-   [<span data-ttu-id="73324-1188">商務用 Skype 的下載及更新</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1188">Skype for Business downloads and updates</span></span>](/SkypeForBusiness/software-updates)

### <a name="devices"></a><span data-ttu-id="73324-1189">裝置</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1189">Devices</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-1190">若要使用麥克風裝置報告，我們需要瞭解平均觀念分數（MOS）的概念。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1190">To make use of the microphone device report, we need to understand the concept of the mean opinion score (MOS).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-1191">MOS 是用來估量所察覺之音訊品質的黃金標準測量。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1191">MOS is the gold-standard measurement to gauge the perceived audio quality.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-1192">它是從0到5的整數評分來表示。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1192">It’s represented as an integer rating from 0 to 5.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-1193">語音品質的所有測量單位都是人員如何感覺語音品質。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1193">The basis of all measures of voice quality is how a person perceives the quality of speech.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-1194">因為它受到人類的認知影響，所以本身就是主觀的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1194">Because it’s affected by human perception, it’s inherently subjective.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-1195">主觀測試有數種不同的方法。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1195">There are several different methodologies for subjective testing.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-1196">大多數的語音品質測量都是以絕對分類評級（ACR）刻度為基礎。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1196">Most voice quality measures are based on an absolute categorization rating (ACR) scale.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-1197">在 ACR 主觀測試中，有統計數量巨大的人員會以1（差）到5（良好）的比例來評定其體驗品質。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1197">In an ACR subjective test, a statistically significant number of people rate their quality of experience on a scale of 1 (bad) to 5 (excellent).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-1198">分數的平均值是 MOS。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1198">The average of the scores is the MOS.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-1199">產生的 MOS 取決於向群組所公開的經驗範圍，以及評級的經驗類型。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1199">The resulting MOS depends on the range of experiences that were exposed to the group and to the type of experience being rated.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-1200">因為對即時通訊系統進行語音品質的主觀測試是不切實際的，所以 Microsoft 團隊和商務用 Skype 會使用高級演算法來產生 MOS 值，以客觀預測主觀測試的結果。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1200">Because it’s impractical to conduct subjective tests of voice quality for a live communication system, Microsoft Teams and Skype for Business generate MOS values by using advanced algorithms to objectively predict the results of a subjective test.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-1201">可用的一組 MOS 及相關的度量單位可提供透過音訊裝置傳送給使用者的體驗品質。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1201">The available set of MOS and associated metrics provide a view into the quality of the experience being delivered to the users by an audio device.</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="73324-1202">您可以為擁有針對小組和商務用 Skype 認證的裝置提供使用者，以減少因裝置本身（例如，內建的膝上型電腦喇叭和麥克風）而遇到負面體驗的可能性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1202">By supplying users with devices certified for Teams and Skype for Business, you reduce the likelihood of encountering negative experiences due to the device itself (which is more likely, for example, with built-in laptop speakers and microphones).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-1203">如需詳細資訊，請參閱[認證計畫](/SkypeForBusiness/certification/overview)和[合作夥伴解決方案目錄](https://partnersolutions.skypeforbusiness.com/solutionscatalog/personal-peripherals-pcs)中的相關文章。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1203">For more information, see these articles on the [certification program](/SkypeForBusiness/certification/overview) and the [partner solutions catalog](https://partnersolutions.skypeforbusiness.com/solutionscatalog/personal-peripherals-pcs).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-1204">裝置報告是用來依音量與 MOS 分數（僅限音訊）來評估裝置使用量，而且可以在 [用戶端 & 裝置] 下的隨附範本中找到。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1204">The device reports are used to assess device usage by volume and MOS score (audio only), and can be found in the accompanying templates under Clients & Devices.</span></span> 

> [!IMPORTANT]
> <span data-ttu-id="73324-1205">除非您排除聯盟參與者資料，否則這些報告將包含來自聯盟端點的用戶端遙測。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1205">Unless you exclude federated participant data, these reports will include client telemetry from federated endpoints.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-1206">若要排除同盟端點，您必須在您組織的[租使用者識別碼](#tenant-id)中，新增**第二個租使用者 id**的查詢篩選器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1206">To exclude federated endpoints, you must add a query filter for **Second Tenant ID** set to your organization’s [tenant ID](#tenant-id).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-1207">或者，您也可以使用[URL 篩選](#url-filter)來排除同盟參與者遙測。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1207">ALternatively, you can use a [URL filter](#url-filter) to exclude federated participant telemetry.</span></span>

> [!NOTE] 
> <span data-ttu-id="73324-1208">請務必將 [月份年份] 篩選調整為 [當月]。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1208">Be sure to adjust the Month Year filter to the current month.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-1209">選取 [**編輯**]，然後調整**月份年份**以儲存新的預設月份。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1209">Select **Edit**, and adjust **Month Year** to save the new default month.</span></span>

> [!Note]
> <span data-ttu-id="73324-1210">您可能會注意到，當您查看此報告時，您會看到多次報告相同的裝置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1210">You might notice when viewing this report that you see the same device reported multiple times.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-1211">這是由於將裝置報告給 CQD 的方式所導致。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1211">This is due to the way the device is reported being reported to CQD.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-1212">硬體與作業系統區域設定的差異會導致報告裝置資料的方式差異。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1212">Differences in hardware and OS locale cause differences in how device data is reported.</span></span>

![裝置（麥克風）報告的螢幕擷取畫面](media/qerguide-image-devicesmicrophone.png)

<span data-ttu-id="73324-1214">_圖 31-裝置（麥克風）報告_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1214">_Figure 31 - Devices (Microphone) Report_</span></span>

##### <a name="remediation"></a><span data-ttu-id="73324-1215">修正</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1215">Remediation</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-1216">通常，您需要探索並階段找出未認證的裝置，並將它們取代為認證的裝置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1216">Typically, you’ll need to discover and phase out non-certified devices and replace them with certified devices.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-1217">查看裝置報告時的一些考慮事項包括：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1217">Some considerations when reviewing the device reports include:</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="73324-1218">適用于團隊和商務用 Skype 的裝置是否已獲認證？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1218">Are the devices in use certified for Teams and Skype for Business?</span></span> 
-   <span data-ttu-id="73324-1219">您可以透過 [[呼叫分析](https://techcommunity.microsoft.com/t5/Skype-for-Business-Blog/Introducing-Call-Analytics/ba-p/57309)] 識別特定裝置的使用者。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1219">You can identify users of a specific device through [Call Analytics](https://techcommunity.microsoft.com/t5/Skype-for-Business-Blog/Introducing-Call-Analytics/ba-p/57309).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-1220">請檢查以確定他們擁有最新的裝置驅動程式，且其裝置未透過 USB 集線器或塢站連接。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1220">Check to make sure they have the latest device drivers and that their device isn’t connected through a USB hub or docking station.</span></span> 
-   <span data-ttu-id="73324-1221">各種不同的驅動程式版本在使用中有多少不同？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1221">How many different versions of various drivers are in use?</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-1222">他們是定期進行修補嗎？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1222">Are they being patched regularly?</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-1223">確保定期修補音訊、影片和 Wi-fi 驅動程式，以協助將這些問題排除在品質問題的來源，並讓使用者體驗更具預見性和一致性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1223">Ensuring that audio, video, and Wi-Fi drivers are being patched regularly will help eliminate these as a source of quality issues and make the user experience more predictable and consistent.</span></span>

##### <a name="audio"></a><span data-ttu-id="73324-1224">音訊</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1224">Audio</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-1225">下一個工作是判斷[認證音訊裝置](https://partnersolutions.skypeforbusiness.com/solutionscatalog/personal-peripherals-pcs)的整體使用量。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1225">The next task is to determine the overall usage of [certified audio devices](https://partnersolutions.skypeforbusiness.com/solutionscatalog/personal-peripherals-pcs).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-1226">我們建議您至少80% 的所有音訊資料流程都使用經過認證的音訊裝置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1226">We recommend that at least 80 percent of all audio streams use a certified audio device.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-1227">最佳做法是將麥克風裝置報告匯出至 Excel，以計算認證或核准裝置的使用方式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1227">This is best accomplished by exporting the microphone devices report to Excel to calculate the usage of certified or approved devices.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-1228">組織通常會保留所有核准裝置的清單，因此篩選及排序資料應該相當簡單。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1228">Organizations typically keep a list of all approved devices, so filtering and sorting the data should be straightforward.</span></span>

##### <a name="video"></a><span data-ttu-id="73324-1229">顯示器</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1229">Video</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-1230">影片驅動程式也很重要，就是繼續更新。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1230">Video drivers are important to keep updated as well.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-1231">確保經常修正的視訊卡，將無法排除視頻驅動程式，因為這是視頻串流品質較差的來源。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1231">Ensuring that video cards are being regularly patched will help exclude video drivers as a source of poor quality for video streams.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-1232">使用[經過驗證的影片裝置](https://partnersolutions.skypeforbusiness.com/solutionscatalog/personal-peripherals-pcs)將有助於確保使用者體驗順暢且高品質。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1232">Using [certified video devices](https://partnersolutions.skypeforbusiness.com/solutionscatalog/personal-peripherals-pcs) will help ensure a smooth and high-quality user experience.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-1233">支援 H-p 原生編碼的視頻裝置是可取的，以減少在視訊會議期間的 CPU 使用量。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1233">Video devices that support H.264 native encoding are preferred, to reduce CPU usage during video conferencing.</span></span>

##### <a name="wi-fi"></a><span data-ttu-id="73324-1234">Wi-fi</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1234">Wi-Fi</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-1235">Wi-fi 驅動程式也必須在一般節奏上進行修補，而且應該包含在您的修補程式管理原則中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1235">Wi-Fi drivers also need to be patched on a regular cadence as well and should be included in your patch management strategy.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-1236">您可以透過維護最新的 Wi-fi 驅動程式來修正許多品質問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1236">Many quality issues can be corrected by maintaining up-to-date Wi-Fi drivers.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-1237">如需優化 Wi-fi 基礎結構的詳細資訊，請參閱[這篇有關 wi-fi 規劃的文章](/skypeforbusiness/certification/networking-wifi)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1237">For more information about optimizing your Wi-Fi infrastructure, see [this article about Wi-Fi planning](/skypeforbusiness/certification/networking-wifi).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-1244">若要將品質與靈活性放入無線網路，Microsoft 的做法有三個部分：端到端規劃、部署中的最佳做法，以及前瞻性維護與運作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1244">Microsoft’s approach to drive quality and agility into the wireless networks comes in three parts: end to end planning, best practices in deployment, and proactive maintenance and operations.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-1245">此解決方案簡述會逐步引導您完成此程式，以確保企業級的商務用 Skype 體驗：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1245">This solution brief walks you through this process to ensure an enterprise-class wireless Skype for Business experience:</span></span>

### <a name="lync-networking-guide"></a><span data-ttu-id="73324-1247">Lync 網路指南</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1247">Lync Networking Guide</span></span>

### <a name="network-performance-requirements"></a><span data-ttu-id="73324-1249">網路效能需求</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1249">Network performance requirements</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-1250">透過 IP 的即時媒體質量（音訊、影片和應用程式共用），會大大受到端對端網路連線的品質影響。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1250">The quality of real-time media (audio, video, and application sharing) over IP is greatly affected by the quality of end-to-end network connectivity.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="73324-1251">針對最佳團隊或商務用 Skype 媒體質量，您的網路必須符合下列網路效能度量單位。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1251">For optimal Teams or Skype for Business media quality, your network must meet the following network performance metrics.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="73324-1252">_資料表 12-網路效能需求_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1252">_Table 12 - Network performance requirements_</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="73324-1253">衡量</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1253">Metric</span></span>                            | <span data-ttu-id="73324-1254">用戶端到 Microsoft Edge</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1254">Client to Microsoft Edge</span></span>           | <span data-ttu-id="73324-1255">客戶邊緣到 Microsoft Edge</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1255">Customer Edge to Microsoft Edge</span></span>    |
|-----------------------------------|------------------------------------|------------------------------------|
| <span data-ttu-id="73324-1256">延遲（一種方式）</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1256">Latency (one way)</span></span>                 | <span data-ttu-id="73324-1257">\<50 ms</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1257">\<50 ms</span></span>                            | <span data-ttu-id="73324-1258">\<30毫秒</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1258">\<30 ms</span></span>                            |
| <span data-ttu-id="73324-1259">延遲（RTT 或往返時間）</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1259">Latency (RTT, or round-trip time)</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="73324-1260">\<100 ms</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1260">\<100 ms</span></span>                           | <span data-ttu-id="73324-1261">\<60 ms</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1261">\<60 ms</span></span>                            |
| <span data-ttu-id="73324-1262">突發資料包遺失</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1262">Burst packet loss</span></span>                 | <span data-ttu-id="73324-1263">\<在任何 200 ms 間隔期間10%</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1263">\<10% during any 200-ms interval</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="73324-1264">\<1% 在任何 200 ms 間隔期間</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1264">\<1% during any 200-ms interval</span></span>    |

| <span data-ttu-id="73324-1268">資料包內部到達抖動</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1268">Packet inter-arrival Jitter</span></span>       | <span data-ttu-id="73324-1269">\<在任何15秒間隔期間30毫秒</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1269">\<30 ms during any 15-sec interval</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="73324-1270">\<在任何15秒間隔期間15毫秒</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1270">\<15 ms during any 15-sec interval</span></span> |
| <span data-ttu-id="73324-1271">資料包重新排序</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1271">Packet reorder</span></span>                    | <span data-ttu-id="73324-1272">\<0.05% 訂單外資料包</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1272">\<0.05% out-of-order packets</span></span>       | <span data-ttu-id="73324-1273">\<0.01% 訂單外資料包</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="73324-1273">\< 0.01% out-of-order packets</span></span>      |
